// ============================================
// SISTEMA DE REPORTAR BUGS (terminal)
// ============================================
function reportBug(context, error) {
    var msg = '🐛 BUG REPORT [v' + BOT_VERSION + ']\n' +
          '📂 Contexto: ' + context + '\n' +
          '❌ Error: ' + (error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)).substring(0, 500) + '\n' +
          (error instanceof Error && error.stack ? '📋 Stack: ' + error.stack.substring(0, 500) + '\n' : '') +
          '🕐 Hora: ' + new Date().toISOString();
    console.log(msg);
}

if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
    window.onerror = function(msg, url, line, col, error) {
        reportBug('window.onerror (linea ' + line + ')', error || msg);
    };
}
try {
    if (typeof process !== 'undefined' && process.on) {
        process.on('uncaughtException', function(err) {
            reportBug('uncaughtException', err);
        });
    }
} catch(e) {}
// Asegurar que la sala no tenga límite de tiempo ni de goles
try { if (typeof room !== 'undefined') { if (room.setTimeLimit) room.setTimeLimit(0); if (room.setScoreLimit) room.setScoreLimit(0); } } catch(e) {}

// SISTEMA VIP (2 NIVELES) - CONFIGURAR AUTH MANUALMENTE
// ============================================
var VIP1_AUTHS = [
    // Agregar auths de jugadores VIP 1 (separados por coma)
    // Ejemplo: 'abc123', 'def456'
];
var VIP2_AUTHS = [
    // Agregar auths de jugadores VIP 2 (separados por coma)
    // VIP 2 tiene todos los beneficios de VIP 1 + extras
    // Ejemplo: 'ghi789'
];

function getVIPLevel(player) {
    var auth = getAuth(player);
    if (!auth) return 0;
    if (VIP2_AUTHS.indexOf(auth) !== -1) return 2;
    if (VIP1_AUTHS.indexOf(auth) !== -1) return 1;
    return 0;
}

// ============================================
// FORMATO DE TEXTO CON UNICODE ESPECIAL
// ============================================
function formatText(text) {
    if (!text) return text;
    var map = {
        'A': 'ᴀ', 'B': 'ʙ', 'C': 'ᴄ', 'D': 'ᴅ', 'E': 'ᴇ', 'F': 'ꜰ', 'G': 'ɢ', 'H': 'ʜ',
        'I': 'ɪ', 'J': 'ᴊ', 'K': 'ᴋ', 'L': 'ʟ', 'M': 'ᴍ', 'N': 'ɴ', 'O': 'ᴏ', 'P': 'ᴘ',
        'Q': 'ǫ', 'R': 'ʀ', 'S': 'ꜱ', 'T': 'ᴛ', 'U': 'ᴜ', 'V': 'ᴠ', 'W': 'ᴡ', 'X': 'x',
        'Y': 'ʏ', 'Z': 'ᴢ',
        'a': 'ᴀ', 'b': 'ʙ', 'c': 'ᴄ', 'd': 'ᴅ', 'e': 'ᴇ', 'f': 'ꜰ', 'g': 'ɢ', 'h': 'ʜ',
        'i': 'ɪ', 'j': 'ᴊ', 'k': 'ᴋ', 'l': 'ʟ', 'm': 'ᴍ', 'n': 'ɴ', 'o': 'ᴏ', 'p': 'ᴘ',
        'q': 'ǫ', 'r': 'ʀ', 's': 'ꜱ', 't': 'ᴛ', 'u': 'ᴜ', 'v': 'ᴠ', 'w': 'ᴡ', 'x': 'x',
        'y': 'ʏ', 'z': 'ᴢ',
        '0': '₀', '1': '₁', '2': '₂', '3': '₃', '4': '₄',
        '5': '₅', '6': '₆', '7': '₇', '8': '₈', '9': '₉'
    };
    var result = '';
    for (var i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {
        result += map[text[i]] || text[i];
    }
    return result;
}

function sendFormatted(room, msg, target, color, style, duration) {
    room.sendAnnouncement(formatText(msg), target, color, style, duration);
}

// Cargar matrimonios de la DB al iniciar
try {
    window.__dbLoadMarriages().then(function(m) {
        if (m && typeof m === 'object') {
            for (var k in m) { botState.marriages[k] = m[k]; }
            var count = Object.keys(m).length / 2;
            if (count > 0) console.log('💍 ' + count + ' matrimonios cargados de la DB');
        }
    }).catch(function(e) { console.log('⚠️ No se pudieron cargar matrimonios'); });
} catch(e) {}

// Cargar datos titan desde DB
try {
    window.__dbLoadTitanData().then(function(data) {
        if (data) {
            botState.titanValues = data.values || {};
            botState.titanTaken = data.taken || [];
            var count = Object.keys(botState.titanValues).length;
            if (count > 0) console.log('📏 ' + count + ' titans cargados de la DB');
        }
    }).catch(function(e) { console.log('⚠️ No se pudieron cargar titans'); });
} catch(e) {}

// Cargar recompensas diarias desde la DB
try {
    window.__dbLoadDailyRewards().then(function(data) {
        if (data && Object.keys(data).length > 0) {
            botState.dailyRewards = data;
            console.log('📅 ' + Object.keys(data).length + ' recompensas diarias cargadas de la DB');
        }
    }).catch(function(e) { console.log('⚠️ No se pudieron cargar recompensas diarias'); });
} catch(e) {}

// ============================================
// SISTEMA DE REPLAYS
// ============================================
function startReplay(gameName) {
    try {
        if (botState.replayRecording) stopReplay();
        room.startRecording();
        botState.replayRecording = true;
        botState.replayGameName = gameName;
        console.log('🎥 Replay iniciado: ' + gameName);
    } catch(e) { console.log('⚠️ Replay start error: ' + e.message); }
}

function stopReplay() {
    if (!botState.replayRecording) return;
    try {
        var data = room.stopRecording();
        botState.replayRecording = false;
        if (data && data.length > 0) {
            var arr = Array.from(data);
            console.log('🎥 Replay detenido: ' + botState.replayGameName + ' (' + arr.length + ' bytes)');
            if (typeof window.__sendReplay === 'function') {
                window.__sendReplay(arr, botState.replayGameName).catch(function(e) {
                    console.log('⚠️ Replay send error: ' + e);
                });
            }
        }
    } catch(e) {
        botState.replayRecording = false;
        console.log('⚠️ Replay stop error: ' + e.message);
    }
}

// Sistema de rangos por victorias (de mayor a menor para buscar el más alto primero)
var RANK_TIERS = [
    { min: 1000, label: '🏆[INMORTAL]',     color: 0xFFD700 },
    { min: 750,  label: '💎[DIVINO]',       color: 0x00FFFF },
    { min: 500,  label: '👑[SUPREMO]',      color: 0xFFD700 },
    { min: 350,  label: '⚡[CELESTIAL]',    color: 0xE6E6FA },
    { min: 250,  label: '🔥[TITAN]',        color: 0xFF0000 },
    { min: 180,  label: '🔥[MITICO]',       color: 0xFF4500 },
    { min: 130,  label: '🔥[LEYENDA]',      color: 0xFF6600 },
    { min: 90,   label: '🟪[GRAN MAESTRO]', color: 0x9400D3 },
    { min: 65,   label: '🟪[MAESTRO]',      color: 0xA020F0 },
    { min: 45,   label: '🟪[ELITE]',        color: 0xBA55D3 },
    { min: 30,   label: '🟦[EXPERTO]',      color: 0x1E90FF },
    { min: 20,   label: '🟦[VETERANO]',     color: 0x4169E1 },
    { min: 12,   label: '🟦[COMPETIDOR]',   color: 0x6495ED },
    { min: 7,    label: '🟫[JUGADOR]',      color: 0xCD853F },
    { min: 3,    label: '🟫[APRENDIZ]',     color: 0xDEB887 },
    { min: 0,    label: '🟫[NOVATO]',       color: 0xD2B48C }
];

function getRankByWins(wins) {
    for (var i = 0; i < RANK_TIERS.length; i++) {
        if (wins >= RANK_TIERS[i].min) {
            return RANK_TIERS[i];
        }
    }
    return RANK_TIERS[RANK_TIERS.length - 1];
}

// Clear bans pero mantener los permanentes
function safeClearBans() {
    try { room.clearBans(); } catch(e){}
    var players = room.getPlayerList();
    var now = Date.now();
    for (var i = 0; i < players.length; i++) {
        var pAuth = players[i].auth || (botState.authMap && botState.authMap[players[i].id]);
        if (!pAuth) continue;
        // Re-kickear bans permanentes
        if (PERMA_BANNED_AUTHS.indexOf(pAuth) !== -1) {
            try { room.kickPlayer(players[i].id, 'Ban permanente', true); } catch(e){}
            continue;
        }
        // Re-kickear temp bans activos
        if (botState.tempBans[pAuth] && botState.tempBans[pAuth].until > now) {
            var secs = Math.ceil((botState.tempBans[pAuth].until - now) / 1000);
            try { room.kickPlayer(players[i].id, 'Ban temporal - ' + secs + 's restantes', true); } catch(e){}
        }
    }
}

// Obtener auth de un jugador (usa authMap porque auth solo está en onPlayerJoin)
function getAuth(player) {
    return player.auth || botState.authMap[player.id] || null;
}

function isMod(player) {
    var auth = getAuth(player);
    return !!(auth && MODERATOR_AUTHS.indexOf(auth) !== -1);
}

// Funcion global para que los modulos puedan filtrar jugadores AFK
function isPlayerAfk(playerId) {
    var pAuth = botState.authMap[playerId] || null;
    return !!(pAuth && botState.afkProtected[pAuth]);
}

function getPlayerTag(player) {
    var auth = getAuth(player);
    var protPrefix = (auth && botState.protectionActive[auth]) ? '🛡️' : '';
    var clanSuffix = (auth && botState.clanTags[auth]) ? ' [' + formatText(botState.clanTags[auth]) + ']' : '';
    // Prioridad: THE BEST > CREADOR > KING > GAY > MVP > RANGO
    if (auth === '1-6gDursmPncJIvqDu_88b-_N2hIeZdUQCsgkGmO2hE') {
        return { label: protPrefix + '⭐[' + formatText('The best') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0x89CFF0 };
    }
    if (auth && CREATOR_AUTHS.indexOf(auth) !== -1) {
        return { label: protPrefix + '⚽[' + formatText('CREADOR') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0x0055FF };
    }
    // Moderadores (color cyan bonito 0x00BFFF)
    if (auth && MODERATOR_AUTHS.indexOf(auth) !== -1) {
        return { label: protPrefix + '🛡️[' + formatText('MOD') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0x00BFFF };
    }
    // VIP+ (nivel 2) - dorado
    if (getVIPLevel({ auth: auth }) === 2) {
        return { label: protPrefix + '🥇[' + formatText('VIP+') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0xFFD700 };
    }
    // VIP (nivel 1) - bronce
    if (getVIPLevel({ auth: auth }) === 1) {
        return { label: protPrefix + '🥉[' + formatText('VIP') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0xCD7F32 };
    }
    if (auth === 'EmnLfhmzGZ0UtP3pjPwAgEyWCNte5yqgwXnvw2qrVic') {
        return { label: protPrefix + '👑[' + formatText('KING') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0xFFFFFF };
    }
    if (auth === 'SpF1TKzWu5U9Xy66vDN8Xk_QCcY0BUmAFID8_uOf11I') {
        return { label: protPrefix + '🔴[' + formatText('LEO') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0xFF0000 };
    }
    if (auth === 'q3qsnVsaZZzr2ZueqLevKtkkJKOL6O6I8DKfiFZA5q4') {
        return { label: protPrefix + '🍀[' + formatText('JUST TGW') + ']🍀' + clanSuffix, color: 0x228B22 };
    }
    if (auth) {
        var tag = botState.playerTags[auth];
        if (tag && tag.remaining > 0) {
            if (tag.type === 'GAY') {
                return { label: protPrefix + '[' + formatText('GAY') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0xFFC0CB };
            }
        }
    }
    if (auth && botState.winStreaks[auth] >= 2) {
        return { label: protPrefix + '[' + formatText('MVP') + ']' + clanSuffix, color: 0xFFD700 };
    }
    // Sistema de rangos por victorias
    var wins = (auth && botState.winsCache[auth]) ? botState.winsCache[auth] : 0;
    var rank = getRankByWins(wins);
    return { label: protPrefix + rank.label + clanSuffix, color: rank.color };
}

function decrementTempTags() {
    for (var auth in botState.playerTags) {
        var tag = botState.playerTags[auth];
        if (tag && tag.remaining > 0) {
            tag.remaining--;
            if (tag.remaining <= 0) {
                delete botState.playerTags[auth];
            }
        }
    }
}

function triggerRandomEvent() {
    var event = RANDOM_EVENTS[Math.floor(Math.random() * RANDOM_EVENTS.length)];
    botState.activeEvent = event;
    room.sendAnnouncement(
        '\n⚡ EVENTO ESPECIAL ⚡\n' + event.name + '\n' + event.description + '\n',
        null, event.color, 'bold', 2
    );
    // Bonus para todos si es ese tipo
    if (event.type === 'bonus_all') {
        var allPlayers = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; });
        allPlayers.forEach(function(p) {
            var pAuth = getAuth(p);
            if (pAuth && typeof window.__dbAddBalance === 'function') {
                try { window.__dbAddBalance(pAuth, p.name, 5000); } catch(e) {}
            }
        });
    }
    // Protección para todos: se maneja en isProtected (igual que no_lucky_ban)
    // No se setea protectionActive individual para evitar que persista entre juegos
}

// ============================================
// SISTEMA ANTI-SPAM
// ============================================
var SPAM_CONFIG = {
    limit: 8,        // mensajes máximos antes de mutear
    window: 6000,    // ventana de tiempo (ms) para contar mensajes
    muteBase: 60000  // duración base del mute (ms): 1 min, 2 min, 3 min...
};

function checkSpam(player) {
    var auth = getAuth(player);
    if (!auth) return false; // sin auth, no se aplica spam
    // CREADORES nunca son muteados
    if (CREATOR_AUTHS.indexOf(auth) !== -1) return false;

    var now = Date.now();
    if (!botState.spamMessages[auth]) botState.spamMessages[auth] = [];

    // Filtrar mensajes fuera de la ventana
    botState.spamMessages[auth] = botState.spamMessages[auth].filter(function(t) {
        return now - t < SPAM_CONFIG.window;
    });
    botState.spamMessages[auth].push(now);

    // Advertencia antes del mute (al llegar a 6 mensajes)
    if (botState.spamMessages[auth].length === SPAM_CONFIG.limit - 2) {
        room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ ' + player.name + ', estás enviando mensajes muy rápido. Si continúas serás muteado.', player.id, 0xFFFF00, 'bold');
    }

    if (botState.spamMessages[auth].length >= SPAM_CONFIG.limit) {
        // Calcular duración del mute (1 min * veces muteado)
        var prevCount = (botState.spamMutes[auth] ? botState.spamMutes[auth].count : 0);
        var muteCount = prevCount + 1;
        var muteDuration = SPAM_CONFIG.muteBase * muteCount;

        botState.spamMutes[auth] = { until: now + muteDuration, count: muteCount };
        botState.spamMessages[auth] = []; // resetear contador

        var minutos = Math.round(muteDuration / 60000);
        room.sendAnnouncement(
            '🔇 ' + player.name + ' fue muteado por ' + minutos + ' minuto(s) por spam.',
            null, 0xFF6600, 'bold'
        );
        room.sendAnnouncement(
            '🔇 Estás muteado por ' + minutos + ' minuto(s) por enviar demasiados mensajes.',
            player.id, 0xFF0000, 'bold'
        );

        // Timer para avisarle cuando se desmutea
        if (botState.spamMuteTimers[auth]) clearTimeout(botState.spamMuteTimers[auth]);
        botState.spamMuteTimers[auth] = setTimeout(function() {
            delete botState.spamMutes[auth];
            delete botState.spamMuteTimers[auth];
            // Buscar al jugador por auth para notificarle
            var players = room.getPlayerList();
            for (var i = 0; i < players.length; i++) {
                if (getAuth(players[i]) === auth) {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('🔊 Ya puedes chatear de nuevo.', players[i].id, 0x00FF00, 'bold');
                    break;
                }
            }
        }, muteDuration);

        return true; // está muteado
    }
    return false;
}

function isSpamMuted(player) {
    var auth = getAuth(player);
    if (!auth) return false;
    if (!botState.spamMutes[auth]) return false;
    return Date.now() < botState.spamMutes[auth].until;
}

// Formatear dinero con separador de miles (estilo $50.000)
function formatMoney(amount) {
    return "$" + amount.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ".");
}

// Buffer de chatlog: acumula mensajes y envía cada 5s para evitar 429
function flushChatlog() {
    if (botState.chatlogBuffer.length === 0) return;
    var batch = botState.chatlogBuffer.splice(0, 20); // max 20 por envío
    var text = batch.join('\n');
    if (text.length > 1900) text = text.substring(0, 1900) + '...';
    if (typeof window.__discordWebhook === 'function') {
        window.__discordWebhook('chatlog', text);
    }
    // Si quedan más, programar otro flush
    if (botState.chatlogBuffer.length > 0) {
        botState.chatlogTimer = setTimeout(flushChatlog, 5000);
    } else {
        botState.chatlogTimer = null;
    }
}

function bufferChatlog(line) {
    botState.chatlogBuffer.push(line);
    if (!botState.chatlogTimer) {
        botState.chatlogTimer = setTimeout(flushChatlog, 5000);
    }
}

// Helper para compras de tienda: verifica saldo, cobra, aplica cooldown
function shopBuy(playerAuth, playerName, playerId, cost, commandName, cooldownMs, callback) {
    if (!playerAuth) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ No se pudo verificar tu identidad', playerId, 0xFF6600); return; }
    var now = Date.now();
    // VIP cooldown reducido: VIP 25%, VIP+ 50%
    var vipLevel = getVIPLevel({ auth: playerAuth });
    var finalCooldown = cooldownMs;
    if (vipLevel === 1) finalCooldown = Math.floor(cooldownMs * 0.75);
    if (vipLevel >= 2) finalCooldown = Math.floor(cooldownMs * 0.50);
    if (finalCooldown > 0) {
        if (!botState.shopCooldowns[playerAuth]) botState.shopCooldowns[playerAuth] = {};
        var last = botState.shopCooldowns[playerAuth][commandName] || 0;
        if (now - last < finalCooldown) {
            var wait = Math.ceil((finalCooldown - (now - last)) / 1000);
            room.sendAnnouncement('⏳ ' + commandName + ' en cooldown. Espera ' + wait + 's', playerId, 0xFF6600);
            return;
        }
    }
    if (typeof window.__dbGetStats !== 'function') { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Tienda no disponible.', playerId, 0xFF6600); return; }
    window.__dbGetStats(playerAuth).then(function(stats) {
        var balance = (stats && stats.balance) ? stats.balance : 0;
        if (balance < cost) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Saldo insuficiente. Necesitas ' + formatMoney(cost) + ' (tienes ' + formatMoney(balance) + ')', playerId, 0xFF6600);
            return;
        }
        try { window.__dbAddBalance(playerAuth, playerName, -cost); } catch(e) {}
        if (finalCooldown > 0) botState.shopCooldowns[playerAuth][commandName] = now;
        callback();
    }).catch(function() { room.sendAnnouncement('❌ Error al verificar saldo.', playerId, 0xFF0000); });
}

// Recompensas del sistema monetario
var moneyConfig = {
    winReward: 2000,         // $2.000 por ganar un minijuego
    streakBonus: 500,        // $500 extra por cada nivel de racha (x2, x3, etc)
    participationReward: 100 // $100 por participar en un minijuego
};

function showGameStats(module) {
    if (module && module.getStats) {
        try {
            var stats = module.getStats();
            if (stats && stats.firstEliminated) {
                room.sendAnnouncement(
                    "⚡ Primer eliminado: " + stats.firstEliminated.name + " (" + stats.firstEliminated.timeS + "s)",
                    null, 0xFF6600
                );
            }
        } catch(e) {}
    }
}

// ============================================
// SISTEMA DE ANUNCIOS AUTOMÁTICOS
// ============================================
function startAutoAnnouncements() {
    setInterval(function() {
        // No enviar anuncios si hay un juego activo (minijuego en curso)
        if (botState.gameActive || botState.chatBlocked) {
            // Marcar anuncio pendiente para enviarlo cuando termine la explicación/minijuego
            botState.pendingAnnouncement = true;
            return; // No enviar anuncios durante juegos activos o cuando el chat está bloqueado
        }
        
        botState.chatBlocked = true;
        
        room.sendAnnouncement(
            "━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n" +
            "💬 ÚNETE A NUESTRO DISCORD\n" +
            "🔗 https://discord.gg/YvFHkSZUvE\n" +
            "━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━",
            null,
            0x5865F2,
            "bold",
            2
        );
        
        setTimeout(function() {
            botState.chatBlocked = false;
        }, 2000);
    }, 120000); // Cada 2 minutos
}

// Vigilar anuncios pendientes y enviarlos cuando sea seguro
function startPendingAnnouncementWatcher() {
    setInterval(function() {
        if (botState.pendingAnnouncement && !botState.gameActive && !botState.chatBlocked) {
            botState.pendingAnnouncement = false;
            botState.chatBlocked = true;
            room.sendAnnouncement(
                "━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n" +
                "💬 ÚNETE A NUESTRO DISCORD\n" +
                "🔗 https://discord.gg/YvFHkSZUvE\n" +
                "━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━",
                null,
                0x5865F2,
                "bold",
                2
            );
            setTimeout(function() { botState.chatBlocked = false; }, 2000);
        }
    }, 2000);
}

// Iniciar watcher de pendientes
startPendingAnnouncementWatcher();

// Iniciar anuncios automáticos
startAutoAnnouncements();

// FUNCIONES PRINCIPALES
// ============================================

// Bloquear cambios de equipo (uso: lockTeamChanges(); unlockTeamChanges();)
// NOTA: room.setTeamsLock(true) ya esta puesto al inicio y NUNCA se desactiva
// Solo usamos botState.teamLock como lock de software para pausas/instrucciones
function lockTeamChanges() {
    botState.teamLock = true;
}
function unlockTeamChanges() {
    botState.teamLock = false;
}

// Manejar kicks/bans realizados desde la UI (click en jugador)
// Firma: onPlayerKicked(kickedPlayer, reason, ban, byPlayer)
room.onPlayerKicked = function(kickedPlayer, reason, ban, byPlayer) {
    try {
        // Trackear kicks y bans en DB
        var kickedAuth = getAuth(kickedPlayer);
        if (kickedAuth && kickedPlayer.name) {
            if (ban) {
                try { window.__dbAddBanCount(kickedAuth, kickedPlayer.name); } catch(e){}
            } else {
                try { window.__dbAddKickCount(kickedAuth, kickedPlayer.name); } catch(e){}
            }
        }

        if (byPlayer && byPlayer.id !== 0) {
            var byAuth = getAuth(byPlayer);
            var isCreator = byAuth && CREATOR_AUTHS.indexOf(byAuth) !== -1;
            // Temp admins NO pueden banear NI kickear
            var isTempAdmin = botState.tempAdmins.indexOf(byPlayer.id) !== -1;
            if (isTempAdmin && !isCreator) {
                if (ban) {
                    safeClearBans();
                }
                try { room.setPlayerAdmin(byPlayer.id, false); } catch(e){}
                var taIdx = botState.tempAdmins.indexOf(byPlayer.id);
                if (taIdx !== -1) botState.tempAdmins.splice(taIdx, 1);
                room.sendAnnouncement('⛔ ' + byPlayer.name + ' abusó del admin temporal. Admin removido.', null, 0xFF0000, 'bold');
                return;
            }

            // permitir a creadores banear
            if (ban) {
                if (!isCreator) {
                    // revertir ban: limpiar bans, quitar admin
                    safeClearBans();
                    try { room.setPlayerAdmin(byPlayer.id, false); } catch(e){}
                    room.sendAnnouncement('⛔ ' + byPlayer.name + ' intentó banear desde la interfaz. Ban revertido y admin removido.', null, 0xFF0000, 'bold');
                }
                return;
            }

            // Si es kick (no ban): aplicar cooldown de 2 minutos por admin (creadores exentos)
            var now = Date.now();
            botState.lastKickBy = botState.lastKickBy || {};
            var last = botState.lastKickBy[byPlayer.id] || 0;
            if (now - last < 120000 && !isCreator) {
                // Violó cooldown: revocar admin temporal y avisar
                try { room.setPlayerAdmin(byPlayer.id, false); } catch(e){}
                room.sendAnnouncement('⛔ Has kickeado demasiado seguido. Tu admin ha sido revocado temporalmente.', byPlayer.id, 0xFF0000, 'bold');
            } else {
                botState.lastKickBy[byPlayer.id] = now;
            }
        }
    } catch (e) { console.error('[ROOM] onPlayerKicked error ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : String(e))); }
};

// Función genérica para iniciar minijuego
function startMinigame(gameEntry) {
    botState.gameActive = true;
    botState.minigameStartTime = Date.now();
    var mod = gameEntry.module;
    if (typeof mod !== 'undefined' && mod.start) {
        // Timeout de seguridad: si el juego no termina en 5 minutos, forzar reinicio
        if (botState.gameSafetyTimeout) clearTimeout(botState.gameSafetyTimeout);
        botState.gameSafetyTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
            if (botState.gameActive) {
                reportBug('startMinigame.safetyTimeout', gameEntry.name + ' no termino en 5 minutos, forzando reinicio');
                forceStopAllGames();
                setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
            }
        }, 300000);
        try {
            mod.start(room, function(winner) {
                if (botState.gameSafetyTimeout) { clearTimeout(botState.gameSafetyTimeout); botState.gameSafetyTimeout = null; }
                if (typeof showGameStats === 'function' && mod) showGameStats(mod);
                console.log('[startMinigame] Callback recibido de ' + gameEntry.name + '. winner=' + (winner ? winner.name + ' (id=' + winner.id + ')' : 'null/undefined'));
                if (winner && winner.id) {
                    loadLuckyMap(winner);
                } else {
                    console.log('[startMinigame] Winner invalido para ' + gameEntry.name + '. Pasando al siguiente juego.');
                    botState.gameActive = false;
                    setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
                }
            });
        } catch(e) {
            reportBug('startMinigame(' + gameEntry.name + ')', e);
            if (botState.gameSafetyTimeout) { clearTimeout(botState.gameSafetyTimeout); botState.gameSafetyTimeout = null; }
            botState.gameActive = false;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
        }
    } else {
        botState.gameActive = false;
        setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
    }
}

function startCOPS_ROBBERS() {
    botState.gameActive = true;
    if (typeof COPS_ROBBERS !== 'undefined') {
        COPS_ROBBERS.start(room, function(result) {
            if (result && result.winningTeam) {
                var players = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; });
                var winnersCount = 0;
                players.forEach(function(p) {
                    if (p.team === result.winningTeam) {
                        var pAuth = getAuth(p);
                        if (pAuth && typeof window.__dbAddBalance === 'function') {
                            try { window.__dbAddBalance(pAuth, p.name, 1000); } catch(e) {}
                        }
                        winnersCount++;
                    }
                });
                room.sendAnnouncement(
                    '\n💰 Cada jugador del equipo ' + result.teamName + ' recibe ' + formatMoney(1000) + '! (' + winnersCount + ' jugadores)',
                    null, 0xFFD700, 'bold', 2
                );
            }
            botState.gameActive = false;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
        });
    } else { botState.gameActive = false; setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000); }
}

function startIMPOSTOR() {
    botState.gameActive = true;
    botState.minigameStartTime = Date.now();
    if (botState.gameSafetyTimeout) clearTimeout(botState.gameSafetyTimeout);
    botState.gameSafetyTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
        if (botState.gameActive) {
            reportBug('startIMPOSTOR.safetyTimeout', 'IMPOSTOR no termino en 5 minutos');
            forceStopAllGames();
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
        }
    }, 300000);

    var savedTempAdmins = botState.tempAdmins.slice();
    for (var ta = 0; ta < savedTempAdmins.length; ta++) {
        var taId = savedTempAdmins[ta];
        try { room.setPlayerAdmin(taId, false); } catch(e) {}
        room.sendAnnouncement('\u26A0\uFE0F Tu admin ha sido removido temporalmente durante IMPOSTOR. Se te devolver\u00E1 al terminar.', taId, 0xFFFF00, 'bold');
    }

    if (typeof IMPOSTOR !== 'undefined' && IMPOSTOR.start) {
        try {
            IMPOSTOR.start(room, function(result) {
                if (botState.gameSafetyTimeout) { clearTimeout(botState.gameSafetyTimeout); botState.gameSafetyTimeout = null; }
                for (var ra = 0; ra < savedTempAdmins.length; ra++) {
                    var raId = savedTempAdmins[ra];
                    var raPlayer = room.getPlayer(raId);
                    if (raPlayer && botState.tempAdmins.indexOf(raId) !== -1) {
                        try { room.setPlayerAdmin(raId, true); } catch(e) {}
                        room.sendAnnouncement('\uD83D\uDC51 Tu admin temporal ha sido restaurado.', raId, 0xFFD700, 'bold');
                    }
                }

                try {
                    if (result && result.type === 'inocentes_win') {
                        for (var i = 0; i < result.inocenteIds.length; i++) {
                            var pAuth = botState.authMap[result.inocenteIds[i]];
                            if (pAuth && typeof window.__dbAddBalance === 'function') {
                                try { window.__dbAddBalance(pAuth, result.inocenteNames[i], 2000); } catch(e) {}
                            }
                        }
                    } else if (result && result.type === 'impostor_win') {
                        var impPrize = (result.impostorIds && result.impostorIds.length === 2) ? 5000 : 10000;
                        if (result.impostorIds) {
                            for (var ii = 0; ii < result.impostorIds.length; ii++) {
                                var impAuth = botState.authMap[result.impostorIds[ii]];
                                var impName = result.impostorNames ? result.impostorNames[ii] : 'Impostor';
                                if (impAuth && typeof window.__dbAddBalance === 'function') {
                                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(impAuth, impName, impPrize); } catch(e) {}
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    } else if (result && result.type === 'bufon_win') {
                        var bufonAuth = botState.authMap[result.bufonId];
                        if (bufonAuth && typeof window.__dbAddBalance === 'function') {
                            try { window.__dbAddBalance(bufonAuth, result.bufonName, 10000); } catch(e) {}
                        }
                    }
                } catch(e) { reportBug('IMPOSTOR.premios', e); }

                botState.gameActive = false;
                setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
            });
        } catch(e) {
            reportBug('startIMPOSTOR', e);
            if (botState.gameSafetyTimeout) { clearTimeout(botState.gameSafetyTimeout); botState.gameSafetyTimeout = null; }
            botState.gameActive = false;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
        }
    } else {
        for (var rb = 0; rb < savedTempAdmins.length; rb++) {
            var rbPlayer = room.getPlayer(savedTempAdmins[rb]);
            if (rbPlayer) { try { room.setPlayerAdmin(savedTempAdmins[rb], true); } catch(e) {} }
        }
        botState.gameActive = false;
        setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
    }
}

// Ban temporal robusto: trackea por auth con timestamp de expiración
function applyTempBan(playerId, duration) {
    var auth = botState.authMap[playerId] || null;
    var player = room.getPlayer(playerId);
    var playerName = player ? player.name : '#' + playerId;

    // Trackear por auth
    if (auth) {
        botState.tempBans[auth] = { until: Date.now() + duration * 1000, name: playerName };
    }

    // Limpiar timer anterior si existe
    if (botState.banTimers[playerId]) clearTimeout(botState.banTimers[playerId]);

    // Agregar a lista legacy de baneados
    if (botState.bannedPlayers.indexOf(playerId) === -1) botState.bannedPlayers.push(playerId);

    // Marcar como kickeado por el juego para que anti-dodge no lo castigue
    if (auth) botState.kickedByGame[auth] = true;

    room.kickPlayer(playerId, 'Ban temporal por ' + duration + 's', true);
    console.log('⚔️ Ban temporal a ' + playerName + ' (auth: ' + auth + ') por ' + duration + 's');

    botState.banTimers[playerId] = setTimeout(function() {
        // Remover de lista legacy
        var index = botState.bannedPlayers.indexOf(playerId);
        if (index !== -1) botState.bannedPlayers.splice(index, 1);
        // Remover de tempBans por auth
        if (auth && botState.tempBans[auth]) delete botState.tempBans[auth];

        safeClearBans();
        room.sendAnnouncement('✅ Ban temporal removido - ' + playerName + ' puede volver a entrar', null, 0x00FF00, 'bold');
        delete botState.banTimers[playerId];
        console.log('✅ Ban temporal removido para ' + playerName);
    }, duration * 1000);
}

// Limpieza periódica de temp bans expirados (cada 15s)
setInterval(function() {
    var now = Date.now();
    var expired = false;
    for (var auth in botState.tempBans) {
        if (botState.tempBans[auth].until <= now) {
            console.log('🔓 Limpieza periódica: ban expirado para ' + botState.tempBans[auth].name);
            delete botState.tempBans[auth];
            expired = true;
        }
    }
    if (expired) safeClearBans();
}, 15000);

// ============================================
// JUICIO PÚBLICO (Ban Vote)
// ============================================
function startBanVote(room, data) {
    // data = { playerId, playerName, auth, duration }
    botState.banVoteActive = true;
    botState.gameActive = true;

    try { room.stopGame(); } catch(e) {}
    try { room.setCustomStadium(mapBanVote); } catch(e) {}

    // Poner acusado en rojo, todos los demás en azul
    var allPlayers = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; });
    var accusedPresent = false;
    allPlayers.forEach(function(p) {
        if (p.id === data.playerId) {
            try { room.setPlayerTeam(p.id, 1); } catch(e) {} // Rojo
            accusedPresent = true;
        } else {
            try { room.setPlayerTeam(p.id, 2); } catch(e) {} // Azul
        }
    });

    // Si el acusado no está, cancelar juicio
    if (!accusedPresent) {
        room.sendAnnouncement('⚖️ El acusado ' + data.playerName + ' se desconectó. Juicio cancelado.', null, 0xFF6600, 'bold');
        botState.banVoteActive = false;
        botState.gameActive = false;
        setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
        return;
    }

    try { room.startGame(); } catch(e) {}
    try { room.pauseGame(true); } catch(e) {}
    botState.chatBlocked = true;

    // Anunciar instrucciones durante la pausa
    room.sendAnnouncement(
        '⚖️ ¡JUICIO PÚBLICO! ⚖️\n' +
        '🔴 Acusado: ' + data.playerName + '\n' +
        '⬆️ Zona ARRIBA = SÍ merece ban\n' +
        '⬇️ Zona ABAJO = NO merece ban\n' +
        '⏱️ Comienza en 5s...',
        null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold', 2
    );

    // Tracking de votos: { playerId: 'ban' | 'noban' }
    var votes = {};
    var voteNames = {};

    // Después de 5s despausar y empezar votación
    botState.banVoteTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
        botState.chatBlocked = false;
        try { room.pauseGame(false); } catch(e) {}
        room.sendAnnouncement('⏱️ ¡15 segundos para votar! Muevan su jugador a la zona.', null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold', 2);

        // Check posiciones cada 500ms
        var checkInterval = setInterval(function() {
            var players = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && p.team === 2; });
            players.forEach(function(p) {
                if (!p.position) return;
                var x = p.position.x;
                var y = p.position.y;

                // Zona "SÍ merece ban": x:65-381, y:-6 a 108
                if (x >= 65 && x <= 381 && y >= -6 && y <= 108) {
                    if (votes[p.id] !== 'ban') {
                        votes[p.id] = 'ban';
                        voteNames[p.id] = p.name;
                        room.sendAnnouncement('✅ ' + p.name + ' votó: SÍ merece ban', null, 0xFF0000, 'bold');
                    }
                }
                // Zona "NO merece ban": x:67-381, y:-174 a -52
                else if (x >= 67 && x <= 381 && y >= -174 && y <= -52) {
                    if (votes[p.id] !== 'noban') {
                        votes[p.id] = 'noban';
                        voteNames[p.id] = p.name;
                        room.sendAnnouncement('❌ ' + p.name + ' votó: NO merece ban', null, 0x00FF00, 'bold');
                    }
                }
            });
        }, 500);

        // Guardar referencia para limpieza
        botState.banVoteInterval = checkInterval;

        // A los 15 segundos, contar votos
        botState.banVoteTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
        clearInterval(checkInterval);
        botState.banVoteInterval = null;

        var banCount = 0;
        var noBanCount = 0;
        for (var pid in votes) {
            if (votes[pid] === 'ban') banCount++;
            else if (votes[pid] === 'noban') noBanCount++;
        }

        room.sendAnnouncement('📊 Resultado: SÍ ban: ' + banCount + ' | NO ban: ' + noBanCount, null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold');

        var verdict;
        if (banCount > noBanCount) {
            verdict = 'ban';
        } else if (noBanCount > banCount) {
            verdict = 'noban';
        } else {
            // Empate o sin votos → aleatorio
            verdict = Math.random() < 0.5 ? 'ban' : 'noban';
            if (banCount === 0 && noBanCount === 0) {
                room.sendAnnouncement('⚖️ ¡Nadie votó! Decidiendo al azar...', null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold');
            } else {
                room.sendAnnouncement('⚖️ ¡EMPATE! Decidiendo al azar...', null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold');
            }
        }

        setTimeout(function() {
            if (verdict === 'ban') {
                room.sendAnnouncement('⚖️ VEREDICTO: ¡CULPABLE! ' + data.playerName + ' será baneado ' + data.duration + 's', null, 0xFF0000, 'bold', 2);
                // Verificar que sigue conectado
                var accused = room.getPlayer(data.playerId);
                if (accused) {
                    applyTempBan(data.playerId, data.duration);
                } else if (data.auth) {
                    // Si se desconectó, guardar ban por auth
                    botState.tempBans[data.auth] = { until: Date.now() + data.duration * 1000, name: data.playerName };
                }
            } else {
                room.sendAnnouncement('⚖️ VEREDICTO: ¡INOCENTE! ' + data.playerName + ' se salva del ban', null, 0x00FF00, 'bold', 2);
            }

            try { room.stopGame(); } catch(e) {}
            botState.banVoteActive = false;
            botState.gameActive = false;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
        }, 2000);
        }, 15000);
    }, 5000);
}

function loadLuckyMap(winner) {
    // Verificar que el ganador es valido (no desconectado, no AFK, no espectador)
    if (winner && winner.id) {
        var winnerCheck = room.getPlayer(winner.id);
        if (!winnerCheck) {
            console.log('⚠️ Ganador ' + winner.name + ' ya no esta en la sala');
            botState.gameActive = false;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
            return;
        }
        // Si el ganador esta en espectador (team 0), anular
        if (winnerCheck.team === 0) {
            console.log('⚠️ Ganador ' + winner.name + ' esta en espectador, anulando victoria');
            botState.gameActive = false;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
            return;
        }
        // Si el ganador tenia spectatorNext, anular esa regla para que juegue el Lucky
        var winnerAuthLucky = getAuth(winnerCheck);
        if (winnerAuthLucky) {
            if (botState.spectatorNext[winnerAuthLucky]) {
                delete botState.spectatorNext[winnerAuthLucky];
            }
            if (botState.spectatorLocked[winnerAuthLucky]) {
                delete botState.spectatorLocked[winnerAuthLucky];
            }
        }
    }
    // Check robo de lucky (!robarlucky) - solo roba el Lucky, no la victoria
    var luckyPlayer = winner;
    if (botState.robarLucky) {
        var thief = room.getPlayer(botState.robarLucky.playerId);
        if (thief) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('🏴‍☠️ ' + botState.robarLucky.name + ' le ROBÓ el Lucky a ' + winner.name + '!', null, 0xFF0000, 'bold', 2);
            luckyPlayer = thief;
        }
        botState.robarLucky = null;
    }

    // Mensaje de victoria aleatorio
    var vMsg = victoryMessages[Math.floor(Math.random() * victoryMessages.length)];
    room.sendAnnouncement(vMsg, null, 0xFFD700, "bold");

    // Obtener auth de forma confiable (auth solo disponible en onPlayerJoin, usar authMap)
    var winnerAuth = (botState.authMap && botState.authMap[winner.id])
        ? botState.authMap[winner.id] : winner.auth;

    // Guardar victoria en DB y actualizar cache de rangos
    if (winnerAuth && typeof window.__dbSaveWin === 'function') {
        try { window.__dbSaveWin(winnerAuth, winner.name, botState.currentMinigame || 'UNKNOWN'); } catch(e) {}
        try { if (typeof window.__dbAddClanWin === 'function') window.__dbAddClanWin(winnerAuth); } catch(e) {}
        var oldWins = botState.winsCache[winnerAuth] || 0;
        var newWins = oldWins + 1;
        botState.winsCache[winnerAuth] = newWins;
        // Verificar si subió de rango
        var oldRank = getRankByWins(oldWins);
        var newRank = getRankByWins(newWins);
        if (oldRank.label !== newRank.label) {
                room.sendAnnouncement(
                    "🎖️ " + formatText(winner.name) + " SUBIO DE RANGO!\n" +
                    formatText(oldRank.label) + " → " + formatText(newRank.label),
                    null, newRank.color, "bold", 2
                );
        }
    }

    // Sistema de rachas
    for (var auth in botState.winStreaks) {
        if (auth !== winnerAuth) {
            delete botState.winStreaks[auth];
        }
    }
    botState.winStreaks[winnerAuth] = (botState.winStreaks[winnerAuth] || 0) + 1;
    var streak = botState.winStreaks[winnerAuth];
    if (streak >= 2) {
        room.sendAnnouncement("🔥 " + formatText(winner.name) + " lleva " + streak + " VICTORIAS SEGUIDAS! 🔥", null, 0xFF4500, "bold", 2);
    } else {
        room.sendAnnouncement("⭐ " + formatText(winner.name) + " — Racha: 1", null, 0xFFAA00);
    }

    // Guardar mejor racha en DB
    if (winnerAuth && typeof window.__dbSaveBestStreak === 'function') {
        try { window.__dbSaveBestStreak(winnerAuth, streak); } catch(e) {}
    }

    // Sistema monetario: recompensa por ganar
    var reward = moneyConfig.winReward;
    var streakBonus = (streak >= 2) ? (streak - 1) * moneyConfig.streakBonus : 0;
    var totalReward = reward + streakBonus;
    // Check !doble: duplicar recompensa si el ganador tiene apuesta activa
    var dobleUsado = false;
    if (winnerAuth && botState.dobleActive[winnerAuth]) {
        totalReward = totalReward * 2;
        dobleUsado = true;
        delete botState.dobleActive[winnerAuth];
    }
    // Bonus matrimonio: +10% si la pareja esta online
    var marriageBonus = false;
    if (winnerAuth && botState.marriages[winnerAuth]) {
        var spouseAuth = botState.marriages[winnerAuth];
        var spouseOnline = room.getPlayerList().find(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && botState.authMap[p.id] === spouseAuth; });
        if (spouseOnline) {
            totalReward = Math.floor(totalReward * 1.10);
            marriageBonus = true;
        }
    }
    // Evento: multiplicador de dinero
    var eventoMulti = '';
    if (botState.activeEvent) {
        if (botState.activeEvent.type === 'double_money') { totalReward = totalReward * 2; eventoMulti = ' (⚡x2 EVENTO!)'; }
        if (botState.activeEvent.type === 'triple_money') { totalReward = totalReward * 3; eventoMulti = ' (⚡x3 EVENTO!)'; }
    }
    // Bonus VIP: +15% VIP 1, +30% VIP 2
    var vipLevel = getVIPLevel({ auth: winnerAuth });
    var vipMulti = '';
    if (vipLevel === 1) {
        totalReward = Math.floor(totalReward * 1.15);
        vipMulti = ' (+15% VIP)';
    } else if (vipLevel === 2) {
        totalReward = Math.floor(totalReward * 1.30);
        vipMulti = ' (+30% VIP+)';
    }
    if (winnerAuth && typeof window.__dbAddBalance === 'function') {
        try { window.__dbAddBalance(winnerAuth, winner.name, totalReward); } catch(e) {}
    }
    var rewardMsg = "💰 " + formatText(winner.name) + " gana " + formatMoney(totalReward);
    if (dobleUsado) {
        rewardMsg += " (x2 DOBLE!)";
    }
    if (eventoMulti) rewardMsg += eventoMulti;
    if (marriageBonus) {
        rewardMsg += " (💍+10%)";
    }
    if (vipMulti) rewardMsg += vipMulti;
    if (streakBonus > 0) {
        rewardMsg += " (+" + formatMoney(streakBonus) + " bonus racha x" + streak + ")";
    }
    room.sendAnnouncement(rewardMsg, null, 0x00FF00, "bold");
    // Limpiar dobles activos de jugadores que no ganaron
    for (var dAuth in botState.dobleActive) {
        if (dAuth !== winnerAuth) delete botState.dobleActive[dAuth];
    }

    room.setPlayerTeam(luckyPlayer.id, 1);

    var allPlayers = room.getPlayerList().filter(p => p.id !== 0);
    allPlayers.forEach(p => {
        if (p.id !== luckyPlayer.id) {
            room.setPlayerTeam(p.id, 0);
        }
    });

    room.sendAnnouncement(
        "\n🎰 PREPARANDO LUCKY...\n🎲 Cargando la ruleta de la suerte...",
        null,
        0xFFD700,
        "bold",
        2
    );
    
    setTimeout(function() {
        stopReplay(); // Enviar replay del minijuego
        try { room.stopGame(); } catch(e) {}
        
        // Verificar que el jugador siga en sala
        var luckyCheck = room.getPlayer(luckyPlayer.id);
        if (!luckyCheck || luckyCheck.team === 0) {
            console.log('⚠️ Lucky player no disponible, saltando...');
            botState.gameActive = false;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
            return;
        }

        try {
            if (!mapLuck) throw new Error('mapLuck no disponible');
            room.setCustomStadium(mapLuck);
            room.startGame();
            startReplay('Lucky - ' + luckyPlayer.name);
            room.setTeamsLock(true);
            console.log('✅ Lucky map cargado correctamente');

            room.sendAnnouncement(
                "🍀 LUCKY MAP - MAPA DE LA SUERTE 🍀\n" +
                "👑 Ganador: " + formatText(winner.name) + (luckyPlayer.id !== winner.id ? ("\n🏴‍☠️ Lucky robado por: " + formatText(luckyPlayer.name)) : "") + "\n" +
                "🎯 Cae en un color y descubre tu destino!",
                null,
                0xFFD700,
                "bold",
                2
            );
            
            console.log("✅ Mapa Lucky cargado correctamente");
            
            // Iniciar detección de colores con callbacks
            LUCKY.start(room, luckyPlayer, function() {
                // Cuando termine Lucky, volver a iniciar otro minijuego
                stopReplay(); // Enviar replay del Lucky
                botState.gameActive = false;
                // Check si hay juicio público pendiente
                if (botState.pendingBanVote) {
                    var voteData = botState.pendingBanVote;
                    botState.pendingBanVote = null;
                    setTimeout(function() { startBanVote(room, voteData); }, 2000);
                } else {
                    setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
                }
            }, {
                isProtected: function(playerId) {
                    // Evento: no ban en lucky o proteccion total
                    if (botState.activeEvent && (botState.activeEvent.type === 'no_lucky_ban' || botState.activeEvent.type === 'protection_all')) return true;
                    // VIP+ (nivel 2) inmune a efectos negativos del Lucky
                    var pAuth = botState.authMap[playerId] || null;
                    if (pAuth && getVIPLevel({ auth: pAuth }) >= 2) {
                        room.sendAnnouncement("🥇 " + (room.getPlayer(playerId) ? room.getPlayer(playerId).name : 'Jugador') + " es VIP+ - ¡INMUNE a efectos negativos!", null, 0xFFD700, "bold", 2);
                        return true;
                    }
                    if (pAuth && botState.protectionActive[pAuth]) {
                        delete botState.protectionActive[pAuth];
                        return true;
                    }
                    return false;
                },
                onProtection: function(playerId) {
                    var pAuth = botState.authMap[playerId] || null;
                    if (pAuth) {
                        botState.protectionActive[pAuth] = true;
                    }
                },
                onReceiveMoney: function(playerId, playerName, amount) {
                    var pAuth = botState.authMap[playerId] || null;
                    if (pAuth && typeof window.__dbAddBalance === 'function') {
                        try { window.__dbAddBalance(pAuth, playerName, amount); } catch(e) {}
                    }
                    console.log("💰 Dinero otorgado: " + playerName + " +$" + amount);
                },
                onSpectatorNext: function(playerId) {
                    // Guardar por AUTH para que no esquiven saliendo/entrando
                    var spAuth = botState.authMap[playerId] || null;
                    if (!spAuth) return;
                    botState.spectatorNext[spAuth] = true;
                    botState.spectatorLocked[spAuth] = true;
                    try { room.sendAnnouncement('👻 Has sido seleccionado para NO jugar el siguiente minijuego', playerId, 0xFF6600, 'bold'); } catch(e){}
                    console.log("👻 Espectador próximo minijuego: auth=" + spAuth);
                    // Desbloqueo automático de seguridad (90s)
                    if (botState.spectatorLockedTimers[spAuth]) clearTimeout(botState.spectatorLockedTimers[spAuth]);
                    botState.spectatorLockedTimers[spAuth] = setTimeout(function() {
                        delete botState.spectatorLocked[spAuth];
                        delete botState.spectatorLockedTimers[spAuth];
                        console.log('🔓 Desbloqueo automático de spectatorLocked para auth=' + spAuth);
                    }, 90000);
                },
                onGayTag: function(playerAuth, playerName) {
                    // Asignar etiqueta GAY por 4 minijuegos
                    botState.playerTags[playerAuth] = { type: 'GAY', remaining: 4 };
                    // Guardar contador en DB
                    if (typeof window.__dbAddGayCount === 'function') {
                        try { window.__dbAddGayCount(playerAuth, playerName || 'Desconocido'); } catch(e) {}
                    }
                    console.log("🌈 Etiqueta GAY asignada a auth: " + playerAuth);
                },
                onBanTemp: function(playerId, duration) {
                    // Check protección antes de banear
                    var pBanAuth = botState.authMap[playerId] || null;
                    if (pBanAuth && botState.protectionActive[pBanAuth]) {
                        delete botState.protectionActive[pBanAuth];
                        var pBanName = (room.getPlayer(playerId) || {name: '#'+playerId}).name;
                        room.sendAnnouncement('🛡️ PROTECCIÓN ACTIVADA! Ban cancelado para ' + pBanName, null, 0x0000FF, 'bold', 2);
                        return;
                    }
                    // 10% probabilidad de juicio público
                    if (Math.random() < 0.10) {
                        var pName = (room.getPlayer(playerId) || {name: '?'}).name;
                        botState.pendingBanVote = { playerId: playerId, playerName: pName, auth: pBanAuth, duration: duration };
                        room.sendAnnouncement('⚖️ ¡Se activó un JUICIO PÚBLICO para ' + pName + '!', null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold', 2);
                        return;
                    }
                    applyTempBan(playerId, duration);
                },
                isAfk: function(playerId) {
                    var pAuth = botState.authMap[playerId] || null;
                    return !!(pAuth && botState.afkProtected[pAuth]);
                },
                onLuckyPass: function(giverId, receiverId) {
                    var giverAuth = botState.authMap[giverId] || null;
                    var receiverAuth = botState.authMap[receiverId] || null;
                    if (!giverAuth || !receiverAuth) return;
                    var now = Date.now();
                    // Limpiar entradas antiguas (>10 min)
                    botState.luckyPassLog = botState.luckyPassLog.filter(function(e) { return now - e.ts < 600000; });
                    // Buscar pase recíproco reciente: ¿receiver le pasó a giver antes?
                    var pairKey = [giverAuth, receiverAuth].sort().join('|');
                    var reciprocal = false;
                    for (var lp = 0; lp < botState.luckyPassLog.length; lp++) {
                        var entry = botState.luckyPassLog[lp];
                        if (entry.giverAuth === receiverAuth && entry.receiverAuth === giverAuth) {
                            reciprocal = true; break;
                        }
                    }
                    // Registrar este pase
                    botState.luckyPassLog.push({ giverAuth: giverAuth, receiverAuth: receiverAuth, ts: now });
                    if (reciprocal) {
                        var giverName = (room.getPlayer(giverId) || {name:'?'}).name;
                        var receiverName = (room.getPlayer(receiverId) || {name:'?'}).name;
                        if (botState.luckyPassWarned[pairKey]) {
                            // Ya fueron advertidos → ban a ambos por 5 minutos
                            room.sendAnnouncement('🚫 ABUSO DETECTADO: ' + giverName + ' y ' + receiverName + ' se están pasando el Lucky entre sí. BAN 5 min para ambos!', null, 0xFF0000, 'bold', 2);
                            applyTempBan(giverId, 300);
                            applyTempBan(receiverId, 300);
                            delete botState.luckyPassWarned[pairKey];
                            // Limpiar log de este par
                            botState.luckyPassLog = botState.luckyPassLog.filter(function(e) {
                                return !((e.giverAuth === giverAuth && e.receiverAuth === receiverAuth) || (e.giverAuth === receiverAuth && e.receiverAuth === giverAuth));
                            });
                        } else {
                            // Primera vez → advertencia
                            botState.luckyPassWarned[pairKey] = true;
                            room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ ADVERTENCIA: ' + giverName + ' y ' + receiverName + ' se están pasando el Lucky entre sí. Si lo hacen de nuevo, ambos serán baneados 5 minutos!', null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold', 2);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        } catch (e) {
            console.log("❌ Error al cargar mapa Lucky: " + e.message);
            botState.gameActive = false;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
        }
    }, 2000);
}

// ============================================
// EXCLUIR JUGADORES AFK DE LOS MINIJUEGOS
// ============================================
function excludeAFKFromGame() {
    // No excluir durante juicio público
    if (botState.banVoteActive || botState.pendingBanVote) return;
    // Si hay un juego activo, no excluir a nadie
    if (botState.gameActive) return;
    // Verificar módulos activos (doble check)
    var anyActive = false;
    try { if (TRIVIA && TRIVIA.isActive && TRIVIA.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (IMPOSTOR && IMPOSTOR.isActive && IMPOSTOR.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (PISTOLERO && PISTOLERO.isActive && PISTOLERO.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (GOT && GOT.isActive && GOT.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (NUMBERCHAIRS && NUMBERCHAIRS.isActive && NUMBERCHAIRS.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (PINBALL_ROULETTE && PINBALL_ROULETTE.isActive && PINBALL_ROULETTE.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (ZOMBIE_RUN && ZOMBIE_RUN.isActive && ZOMBIE_RUN.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (BUHO && BUHO.isActive && BUHO.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (BASKETBALL && BASKETBALL.isActive && BASKETBALL.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (CHARGE && CHARGE.isActive && CHARGE.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (RUN_MINI && RUN_MINI.isActive && RUN_MINI.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (WAR_CONQUEST && WAR_CONQUEST.isActive && WAR_CONQUEST.isActive()) anyActive = true; } catch(e){}
    if (anyActive) return;
    // En modo test no excluir por AFK
    if (typeof TEST_ONLY_GAMES !== 'undefined' && TEST_ONLY_GAMES && TEST_ONLY_GAMES.length > 0) return;
    var now = Date.now();
    var players = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; });
    // Resetear timers de AFK - jugadores que acaban de terminar un juego no deben ser penalizados
    for (var ri = 0; ri < players.length; ri++) {
        botState.afkLastActivity[players[ri].id] = now;
    }
    players.forEach(function(p) {
        var auth = getAuth(p);
        // Excluir si uso !afk
        if (auth && botState.afkProtected[auth]) {
            try { room.setPlayerTeam(p.id, 0); } catch(e) {}
            return;
        }
    });
}

// ============================================
// DETENER TODOS LOS JUEGOS (helper reutilizable)
// ============================================
function forceStopAllGames() {
    stopReplay();
    if (botState.banVoteActive) {
        if (botState.banVoteInterval) { clearInterval(botState.banVoteInterval); botState.banVoteInterval = null; }
        if (botState.banVoteTimeout) { clearTimeout(botState.banVoteTimeout); botState.banVoteTimeout = null; }
        botState.banVoteActive = false;
        botState.chatBlocked = false;
    }
    botState.pendingBanVote = null;
    minigameModules.forEach(function(g) {
        try { if (g.module && g.module.isActive && g.module.isActive()) g.module.stop(room); } catch(e) { reportBug('forceStopAllGames.stop(' + g.name + ')', e); }
    });
    // Lucky modules (separados por lógica especial)
    try { if (LUCKY.isActive()) LUCKY.stop(room); } catch(e){}
    try { if (LUCKY_HELL && LUCKY_HELL.isActive && LUCKY_HELL.isActive()) LUCKY_HELL.stop(room); } catch(e){}
    try { if (LUCKY_DIOS && LUCKY_DIOS.isActive && LUCKY_DIOS.isActive()) LUCKY_DIOS.stop(room); } catch(e){}
    try { room.stopGame(); } catch(e){}
    room.onTeamGoal = gameGoalHandler;
    botState.gameActive = false;
    if (botState.gameSafetyTimeout) { clearTimeout(botState.gameSafetyTimeout); botState.gameSafetyTimeout = null; }
    if (botState.startTimeout) {
        clearTimeout(botState.startTimeout);
        botState.startTimeout = null;
    }
}

function checkAndStart() {
    // Si hay un juicio público en curso, no iniciar
    if (botState.banVoteActive) {
        botState.startTimeout = setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
        return;
    }
    // Si hay un Lucky activo (normal, DIOS o HELL), no iniciar el siguiente minijuego
    if (LUCKY.isActive() || LUCKY_DIOS.isActive() || LUCKY_HELL.isActive()) {
        botState.startTimeout = setTimeout(checkAndStart, 5000);
        return;
    }

    if (botState.gameActive) return;

    // Safety: verificar que ningún módulo de juego siga activo (race condition)
    var anyModuleActive = false;
    minigameModules.forEach(function(g) {
        try { if (g.module && g.module.isActive && g.module.isActive()) anyModuleActive = true; } catch(e){}
    });
    if (anyModuleActive) {
        console.log('⚠️ Safety: módulo de juego aún activo, forzando stop');
        forceStopAllGames();
        botState.startTimeout = setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
        return;
    }

    if (botState.startTimeout) {
        clearTimeout(botState.startTimeout);
        botState.startTimeout = null;
    }
    
    var playerCount = room.getPlayerList().filter(p => p.id !== 0).length;
    
    if (playerCount < 2) {
        room.sendAnnouncement(
            "⏳ Esperando más jugadores... (mínimo 2)",
            null,
            0xFFFF00
        );
        if (playerCount === 1) startSoloEntertainment();
        botState.startTimeout = setTimeout(checkAndStart, 10000);
    } else {
        stopSoloEntertainment();
        // Mover jugadores AFK a espectadores antes de iniciar juego
        excludeAFKFromGame();
        // Decrementar etiquetas temporales al iniciar nuevo minijuego
        decrementTempTags();

        // Procesar inversiones activas
        for (var invAuth in botState.inversiones) {
            var inv = botState.inversiones[invAuth];
            inv.gamesLeft--;
            if (inv.gamesLeft <= 0) {
                // Resolver inversion
                var roll = Math.random() * 100;
                var multiplier, resultMsg;
                if (roll < 15) { multiplier = 0; resultMsg = '💥 QUIEBRA! Perdiste toda tu inversion'; }
                else if (roll < 40) { multiplier = 0.5; resultMsg = '📉 Mala suerte... recuperas solo la mitad'; }
                else if (roll < 65) { multiplier = 1; resultMsg = '📊 Recuperas tu inversion (x1)'; }
                else if (roll < 82) { multiplier = 1.5; resultMsg = '📈 Ganancia moderada! x1.5'; }
                else if (roll < 92) { multiplier = 2; resultMsg = '🚀 Buena inversion! x2'; }
                else if (roll < 97) { multiplier = 3; resultMsg = '🎰 Gran inversion! x3'; }
                else { multiplier = 4; resultMsg = '💎 JACKPOT! x4!!'; }
                var pago = Math.floor(inv.monto * multiplier);
                if (pago > 0) {
                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(invAuth, inv.name, pago); } catch(e) {}
                }
                var colorRes = multiplier >= 2 ? 0x00FF00 : (multiplier >= 1 ? 0xFFFF00 : 0xFF0000);
                room.sendAnnouncement('📈 INVERSION de ' + inv.name + ' maduro!\n' + resultMsg + '\nInvirtio: ' + formatMoney(inv.monto) + ' → Recibe: ' + formatMoney(pago), null, colorRes, 'bold', 2);
                delete botState.inversiones[invAuth];
            } else {
                // Buscar jugador online para notificar
                var invPlayer = room.getPlayerList().find(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && botState.authMap[p.id] === invAuth; });
                if (invPlayer) {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('📈 Tu inversion de ' + formatMoney(inv.monto) + ' madura en ' + inv.gamesLeft + ' juegos', invPlayer.id, 0x00BFFF);
                }
            }
        }

        // Procesar prestamos activos - SISTEMA DESACTIVADO
        if (false) for (var prestAuth in botState.prestamos) {
            var prest = botState.prestamos[prestAuth];
            prest.gamesLeft--;
            var prestPlayer = room.getPlayerList().find(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && botState.authMap[p.id] === prestAuth; });
            if (prest.gamesLeft > 0) {
                // Todavia tiene tiempo
                if (prestPlayer && prest.gamesLeft <= 5) {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('🏦 Te quedan ' + prest.gamesLeft + ' juegos para pagar tu prestamo de ' + formatMoney(prest.deudaTotal), prestPlayer.id, 0xFFFF00);
                }
            } else {
                // Se acabo el tiempo, cobrar interes
                prest.intereses++;
                prest.deudaTotal += 5000;
                if (prest.intereses >= 5) {
                    // 5 intereses sin pagar → saldo a 0 y eliminar prestamo
                    try { window.__dbGetStats(prestAuth).then(function(stats) {
                        var bal = (stats && stats.balance) ? stats.balance : 0;
                        if (bal > 0) { try { window.__dbAddBalance(prestAuth, prest.name, -bal); } catch(e) {} }
                    }); } catch(e) {}
                    room.sendAnnouncement('🏦💀 ' + prest.name + ' no pago su prestamo! Saldo confiscado a $0', null, 0xFF0000, 'bold', 2);
                    delete botState.prestamos[prestAuth];
                } else {
                    // Cobrar interes de $5.000
                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(prestAuth, prest.name, -5000); } catch(e) {}
                    room.sendAnnouncement('🏦 INTERES #' + prest.intereses + '/5 cobrado a ' + prest.name + ': -' + formatMoney(5000) + ' | Deuda total: ' + formatMoney(prest.deudaTotal) + (prestPlayer ? '' : ' (offline)'), null, 0xFF6600, 'bold');
                    if (prestPlayer) {
                        room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Paga con !pagar [monto] o perderas todo tu saldo al interes #5', prestPlayer.id, 0xFF0000);
                    }
                    // Darle 5 juegos mas para pagar antes del siguiente interes
                    prest.gamesLeft = 5;
                }
            }
        }

        // Procesar prestamos P2P - SISTEMA DESACTIVADO
        if (false) (function() {
            var p2pKeys = Object.keys(botState.prestamosP2P);
            for (var pi = 0; pi < p2pKeys.length; pi++) {
                var dAuth = p2pKeys[pi];
                var p2p = botState.prestamosP2P[dAuth];
                if (p2p.cuotasPagadas >= p2p.cuotasTotales) {
                    // Prestamo completado
                    if (botState.prestamistas[p2p.prestamistaAuth]) {
                        botState.prestamistas[p2p.prestamistaAuth].totalGanado += (p2p.montoTotal - p2p.monto);
                    }
                    room.sendAnnouncement('🤝✅ ' + p2p.deudorNombre + ' termino de pagar su prestamo personal a ' + p2p.prestamistaNombre + '!', null, 0x00FF00, 'bold', 2);
                    delete botState.prestamosP2P[dAuth];
                    continue;
                }
                // Intentar cobrar cuota
                var deudorPlayer = room.getPlayerList().find(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && botState.authMap[p.id] === dAuth; });
                (function(deudorAuth, prest) {
                    if (typeof window.__dbGetStats !== 'function') return;
                    window.__dbGetStats(deudorAuth).then(function(stats) {
                        var bal = (stats && stats.balance) ? stats.balance : 0;
                        if (bal >= prest.cuotaMonto) {
                            // Cobrar cuota
                            try { window.__dbAddBalance(deudorAuth, prest.deudorNombre, -prest.cuotaMonto); } catch(e) {}
                            try { window.__dbAddBalance(prest.prestamistaAuth, prest.prestamistaNombre, prest.cuotaMonto); } catch(e) {}
                            prest.cuotasPagadas++;
                            prest.impagos = 0;
                            var restantes = prest.cuotasTotales - prest.cuotasPagadas;
                            var dp = room.getPlayerList().find(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && botState.authMap[p.id] === deudorAuth; });
                            if (dp) {
                                room.sendAnnouncement('🤝 Cuota #' + prest.cuotasPagadas + '/' + prest.cuotasTotales + ' pagada a ' + prest.prestamistaNombre + ': -' + formatMoney(prest.cuotaMonto) + ' | Restante: ' + (restantes > 0 ? restantes + ' cuotas' : 'COMPLETADO!'), dp.id, 0x00BFFF);
                            }
                            if (prest.cuotasPagadas >= prest.cuotasTotales) {
                                if (botState.prestamistas[prest.prestamistaAuth]) {
                                    botState.prestamistas[prest.prestamistaAuth].totalGanado += (prest.montoTotal - prest.monto);
                                }
                                room.sendAnnouncement('🤝✅ ' + prest.deudorNombre + ' termino de pagar su prestamo personal a ' + prest.prestamistaNombre + '!', null, 0x00FF00, 'bold', 2);
                                delete botState.prestamosP2P[deudorAuth];
                            }
                        } else {
                            // No tiene saldo
                            prest.impagos++;
                            prest.deudaPendiente += prest.cuotaMonto;
                            var dp2 = room.getPlayerList().find(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && botState.authMap[p.id] === deudorAuth; });
                            if (dp2) {
                                room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Impago #' + prest.impagos + '/10 - No tienes saldo para la cuota de ' + formatMoney(prest.cuotaMonto) + '. Paga con !pagarp2p', dp2.id, 0xFF6600);
                            }
                            if (prest.impagos >= 10) {
                                // Confiscar saldo del deudor
                                if (bal > 0) {
                                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(deudorAuth, prest.deudorNombre, -bal); } catch(e) {}
                                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(prest.prestamistaAuth, prest.prestamistaNombre, bal); } catch(e) {}
                                }
                                // Devolver monto original del prestamo al prestamista
                                var montoDevolver = prest.monto - (prest.cuotasPagadas * prest.cuotaMonto);
                                if (montoDevolver > 0) {
                                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(prest.prestamistaAuth, prest.prestamistaNombre, montoDevolver); } catch(e) {}
                                }
                                room.sendAnnouncement('🤝💀 ' + prest.deudorNombre + ' acumulo 10 impagos! Saldo confiscado + $' + formatMoney(montoDevolver > 0 ? montoDevolver : 0) + ' devueltos a ' + prest.prestamistaNombre + '. Prestamo cerrado.', null, 0xFF0000, 'bold', 2);
                                delete botState.prestamosP2P[deudorAuth];
                            }
                        }
                    }).catch(function() {});
                })(dAuth, p2p);
            }
        })();

        // SISTEMA DE MINIJUEGOS ALEATORIOS (evitar repetir el último)
        // Lista completa de minijuegos disponibles
        var minigames = minigameModules.slice();

        // Modo test: filtrar solo los juegos seleccionados
        if (typeof TEST_ONLY_GAMES !== 'undefined' && TEST_ONLY_GAMES && TEST_ONLY_GAMES.length > 0) {
            minigames = minigames.filter(function(g) {
                return TEST_ONLY_GAMES.indexOf(g.name) !== -1;
            });
            console.log("🧪 TEST: Solo jugando " + minigames.map(function(g){ return g.name; }).join(", "));
        }

        // ============================================
        // SISTEMA DE BOLSA: jugar todos antes de repetir
        // ============================================
        // Filtrar minijuegos que NO se pueden jugar por cantidad de jugadores
        function filterByPlayerCount(gameList) {
            return gameList.filter(function(game) {
                if (game.name === 'DODGEBALL' && playerCount < 3) return false;
                if (game.name === 'CHAIRMIX' && playerCount < 8) return false;
                if (game.name === 'SURVIVAL' && playerCount > 21) return false;
                if (game.name === 'METEORS' && playerCount > 15) return false;
                if (game.name === 'RING_SURVIVAL' && playerCount > 20) return false;
                if (game.name === 'COPS_ROBBERS' && playerCount < 4) return false;
                if (game.name === 'WWECROSS' && playerCount > 12) return false;
                if (game.name === 'IMPOSTOR' && playerCount < 4) return false;
                if (game.name === 'PISTOLERO' && playerCount < 4) return false;
                if (game.name === 'BUHO' && playerCount > 16) return false;
                if (game.name === 'BUHO' && playerCount < 3) return false;
                return true;
            });
        }

        // Check !elegir: si alguien eligió el próximo juego, usarlo
        var selectedGame = null;
        var selectedIndex = -1;
        if (botState.chosenNextGame) {
            var chosen = minigames.find(function(g) { return g.name === botState.chosenNextGame.name; });
            if (chosen) {
                selectedGame = chosen;
                if (botState.chosenNextGame.isBites) {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('💣 BITES THE DUST — Repitiendo: ' + formatText(chosen.displayName), null, 0xFF69B4, 'bold', 2);
                } else {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('🎯 ' + formatText(botState.chosenNextGame.playerName) + ' eligió el próximo juego: ' + formatText(chosen.displayName), null, 0x00BFFF, 'bold', 2);
                }
            }
            botState.chosenNextGame = null;
        }

        // Si la bolsa esta vacia o no existe, rellenarla con todos los minijuegos (mezclados)
        if (!selectedGame && (!botState.minigameBag || botState.minigameBag.length === 0)) {
            botState.minigameBag = minigames.map(function(g) { return g.name; });
            // Mezclar la bolsa (Fisher-Yates)
            for (var i = botState.minigameBag.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
                var j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
                var tmp = botState.minigameBag[i];
                botState.minigameBag[i] = botState.minigameBag[j];
                botState.minigameBag[j] = tmp;
            }
            console.log("🎲 Nueva bolsa de minijuegos: " + botState.minigameBag.join(", "));
        }

        // Buscar el primer juego de la bolsa que sea jugable (si no fue elegido por !elegir)
        if (!selectedGame) {
        for (var i = 0; i < botState.minigameBag.length; i++) {
            var gameName = botState.minigameBag[i];
            // No repetir el ultimo jugado
            if (gameName === botState.lastMinigame) continue;
            // Buscar en la lista de minijuegos
            var gameObj = minigames.find(function(g) { return g.name === gameName; });
            if (!gameObj) continue;
            // Verificar restricciones de jugadores
            if (gameName === 'DODGEBALL' && playerCount < 3) continue;
            if (gameName === 'CHAIRMIX' && playerCount < 8) continue;
            if (gameName === 'SURVIVAL' && playerCount > 21) continue;
            if (gameName === 'METEORS' && playerCount > 15) continue;
            if (gameName === 'RING_SURVIVAL' && playerCount > 20) continue;
            if (gameName === 'COPS_ROBBERS' && playerCount < 4) continue;
            if (gameName === 'WWECROSS' && playerCount > 12) continue;
            if (gameName === 'IMPOSTOR' && playerCount < 4) continue;
            if (gameName === 'PISTOLERO' && playerCount < 4) continue;
            selectedGame = gameObj;
            selectedIndex = i;
            break;
        }

        // Si no se encontro ninguno jugable, rellenar la bolsa y tomar cualquiera valido
        if (!selectedGame) {
            var available = filterByPlayerCount(minigames).filter(function(g) {
                return g.name !== botState.lastMinigame;
            });
            if (available.length === 0) {
                available = filterByPlayerCount(minigames);
            }
            selectedGame = available[Math.floor(Math.random() * available.length)];
            // Resetear la bolsa
            botState.minigameBag = [];
        } else {
            // Remover el juego seleccionado de la bolsa
            botState.minigameBag.splice(selectedIndex, 1);
        }
        } // fin if (!selectedGame)
        
        console.log('🎮 Juego seleccionado: ' + selectedGame.name + ' | lastMinigame: ' + botState.lastMinigame + ' | bolsa restante: ' + botState.minigameBag.length);
        botState.lastMinigame = selectedGame.name;
        botState.currentMinigame = selectedGame.name;
        botState.gameActive = true; // Marcar activo INMEDIATAMENTE para evitar duplicados
        botState.bitesUsedThisGame = false; // Reset bites the dust para nuevo juego
        botState.minigameStartTime = Date.now(); // Timestamp de inicio
        // Decrementar cooldown de poderes por jugador
        for (var pcAuth in botState.powerCooldownGames) {
            botState.powerCooldownGames[pcAuth]--;
            if (botState.powerCooldownGames[pcAuth] <= 0) delete botState.powerCooldownGames[pcAuth];
        }
        // Decrementar cooldown de !elegir por jugador
        for (var ecAuth in botState.elegirCooldownGames) {
            botState.elegirCooldownGames[ecAuth]--;
            if (botState.elegirCooldownGames[ecAuth] <= 0) delete botState.elegirCooldownGames[ecAuth];
        }

        // Sistema de eventos aleatorios
        botState.activeEvent = null; // limpiar evento anterior
        if (botState.gamesUntilEvent <= 0) {
            botState.gamesUntilEvent = 4 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 5); // próximo en 4-8 juegos
            triggerRandomEvent();
        } else {
            botState.gamesUntilEvent--;
        }

        // Incrementar gamesPlayed para todos los jugadores presentes
        var currentPlayers = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; });
        currentPlayers.forEach(function(p) {
            var pAuth = getAuth(p);
            if (pAuth) {
                botState.gamesPlayed[pAuth] = (botState.gamesPlayed[pAuth] || 0) + 1;
                // Guardar en DB
                if (typeof window.__dbSaveGamePlayed === 'function') {
                    try { window.__dbSaveGamePlayed(pAuth, p.name); } catch(e) {}
                }
                // Recompensa por participar
                if (typeof window.__dbAddBalance === 'function') {
                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(pAuth, p.name, moneyConfig.participationReward); } catch(e) {}
                }
            }
        });

        // Anuncio del minijuego + cuenta regresiva
        room.sendAnnouncement(
            "🎲 Proximo: " + selectedGame.displayName + "\n👥 Jugadores: " + playerCount,
            null, 0x00BFFF, "bold", 2
        );
        setTimeout(function() { room.sendAnnouncement("⏱️ 3...", null, 0xFFFF00, "bold", 2); }, 500);
        setTimeout(function() { room.sendAnnouncement("⏱️ 2...", null, 0xFFA500, "bold", 2); }, 1500);
        setTimeout(function() { room.sendAnnouncement("⏱️ 1...", null, 0xFF6600, "bold", 2); }, 2500);

        // Aplicar spectactorNext SOLO para el próximo minijuego: mover a espectador ahora y limpiar la lista
        // Aplicar spectatorNext por auth: mover a espectador
        if (botState.spectatorNext && Object.keys(botState.spectatorNext).length > 0) {
            var allP = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; });
            allP.forEach(function(p) {
                var pAuth = getAuth(p);
                if (pAuth && botState.spectatorNext[pAuth]) {
                    try { room.setPlayerTeam(p.id, 0); } catch(e){}
                }
            });
            botState.spectatorNext = {};
        }
        // VIP+: dar protección gratis al iniciar juego (1 vez por juego)
        var vipProtecGiven = {};
        var allPlayersNow = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; });
        allPlayersNow.forEach(function(p) {
            var pAuth = getAuth(p);
            if (pAuth && getVIPLevel({ auth: pAuth }) >= 2 && !vipProtecGiven[pAuth]) {
                botState.protectionActive[pAuth] = true;
                vipProtecGiven[pAuth] = true;
                room.sendAnnouncement('🥇 ' + formatText(p.name) + ' recibe protección VIP+ gratis!', null, 0xFFD700);
            }
        });
        botState.startTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
            startReplay(selectedGame.displayName);
            startMinigame(selectedGame);
        }, 3500);
    }
}

// ============================================
// SISTEMA DE ESPERA PARA JUGADOR SOLO
// ============================================
var soloMessages = [
    "💡 Sabías que puedes ver tu rango con !stats?",
    "💡 Usa !discord para unirte a la comunidad!",
    "💡 El ganador de cada minijuego gana $50.000!",
    "💡 Si llevas racha de victorias, ganas bonus extra!",
    "💡 Usa !top para ver a los mejores jugadores!",
    "💡 Hay 30 minijuegos diferentes en esta sala!",
    "💡 Los rangos van desde Novato hasta Titan!",
    "💡 Puedes transferir dinero a otros con !pasar!",
