            typeof CAPTURE_THE_FLAG !== 'undefined' && CAPTURE_THE_FLAG,
            typeof FUTBOL_CALLEJERO !== 'undefined' && FUTBOL_CALLEJERO,
            typeof PLUM !== 'undefined' && PLUM,
            typeof GOL_A_GOL !== 'undefined' && GOL_A_GOL
        ];
        for (var _bg = 0; _bg < _btdGoalGames.length; _bg++) {
            try { if (_btdGoalGames[_bg] && _btdGoalGames[_bg].isActive && _btdGoalGames[_bg].isActive()) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ No puedes usar !bitesthedust en juegos de gol', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; } } catch(e){}
        }
        if (botState.bitesUsedThisGame) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Ya se uso Bites the Dust en este minijuego', player.id, 0xFF6600);
            return false;
        }
        var btdNow = Date.now();
        var btdElapsed = btdNow - (botState.minigameStartTime || 0);
        if (btdElapsed > 10000) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Bites the Dust solo se puede usar en los primeros 10 segundos del minijuego', player.id, 0xFF6600);
            return false;
        }
        if (btdNow < botState.bitesGlobalCooldown) {
            var btdWait = Math.ceil((botState.bitesGlobalCooldown - btdNow) / 1000);
            room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Bites the Dust en cooldown global. Espera ' + btdWait + 's', player.id, 0xFF6600);
            return false;
        }
        if (playerAuth && botState.powerCooldownGames[playerAuth] > 0) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Poderes en cooldown. Faltan ' + botState.powerCooldownGames[playerAuth] + ' partidas', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        shopBuy(playerAuth, player.name, player.id, 35000, '!bitesthedust', 0, function() {
            if (playerAuth) botState.powerCooldownGames[playerAuth] = 5;
            botState.bitesUsedThisGame = true;
            botState.bitesGlobalCooldown = Date.now() + 600000; // 10 min global
            room.sendAnnouncement(
                '\n' +
                '[ KILLER QUEEN: BITES THE DUST ]\n' +
                player.name + ' ha activado Bites the Dust!\n' +
                'El tiempo se rebobina... La ronda se reinicia!\n',
                null, 0xFF69B4, 'bold', 2
            );
            // Reiniciar: parar el juego y volver a iniciar
            var currentGame = botState.currentMinigame;
            setTimeout(function() {
                forceStopAllGames();
                botState.gameActive = false;
                botState.bitesUsedThisGame = true; // mantener el flag
                setTimeout(function() {
                    // Re-seleccionar el mismo juego
                    botState.chosenNextGame = { name: currentGame, playerName: 'Bites the Dust', isBites: true };
                    checkAndStart();
                }, 2000);
            }, 2000);
        });
        return false;
    }

    // !diario - Recompensa diaria por conectarse (racha 7 dias)
    if (message === '!diario') {
        var diarioNow = Date.now();
        if (!botState.dailyRewards[playerAuth]) {
            botState.dailyRewards[playerAuth] = { lastClaim: 0, streak: 0 };
        }
        var dr = botState.dailyRewards[playerAuth];
        var msSinceLast = diarioNow - dr.lastClaim;
        var hours24 = 86400000;
        var hours48 = 172800000;
        if (msSinceLast < hours24) {
            var horasRestantes = Math.ceil((hours24 - msSinceLast) / 3600000);
            room.sendAnnouncement('⏳ Ya reclamaste tu recompensa diaria. Vuelve en ' + horasRestantes + ' hora(s)', player.id, 0xFF6600);
            return false;
        }
        // Si pasaron mas de 48h, se pierde la racha
        if (msSinceLast > hours48) dr.streak = 0;
        dr.streak = Math.min(dr.streak + 1, 7);
        dr.lastClaim = diarioNow;
        // Guardar en DB para persistencia
        try { window.__dbSaveDailyReward(playerAuth, dr.lastClaim, dr.streak); } catch(e) {}
        var premiosDiarios = [1000, 2000, 3000, 4000, 5000, 7000, 10000];
        var premioDiario = premiosDiarios[dr.streak - 1];
        try { window.__dbAddBalance(playerAuth, player.name, premioDiario); } catch(e) {}
        var streakMsg = '';
        for (var sd = 1; sd <= 7; sd++) {
            streakMsg += (sd <= dr.streak ? '🟢' : '⚫');
        }
        room.sendAnnouncement('📅 RECOMPENSA DIARIA - Dia ' + dr.streak + '/7\n' + streakMsg + '\n💰 +' + formatMoney(premioDiario) + (dr.streak === 7 ? ' RACHA COMPLETA!' : ''), player.id, 0x00FF00, 'bold', 2);
        return false;
    }

    // !crash [monto] - Multiplicador que sube, retiras cuando quieras (cooldown 60s)
    if (message.startsWith('!crash') && !botState.crashActive) {
        if (_apuestasBloqueadas) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Espera a que termine la ronda actual', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
    }
    if (message.startsWith('!crash')) {
        var crashParts = message.split(' ');
        // Si hay crash activo y escribe !crash, retirar
        if (botState.crashActive && botState.crashActive.auth === playerAuth && !botState.crashActive.crashed) {
            var cashout = Math.floor(botState.crashActive.monto * botState.crashActive.multiplier);
            clearInterval(botState.crashActive.interval);
            try { window.__dbAddBalance(playerAuth, player.name, cashout); } catch(e) {}
            room.sendAnnouncement('💰 ' + player.name + ' se retiro en x' + botState.crashActive.multiplier.toFixed(2) + '! Gana ' + formatMoney(cashout), null, 0x00FF00, 'bold', 2);
            botState.crashActive = null;
            return false;
        }
        if (crashParts.length < 2) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('🚀 Usa: !crash [monto]\nEl multiplicador sube (x1.1, x1.5, x2...).\nEscribe !crash para retirar antes de que crashee!\nSi crashea, pierdes todo.', player.id, 0xFFFF00);
            return false;
        }
        if (botState.crashActive) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Ya hay un crash activo', player.id, 0xFF6600);
            return false;
        }
        var crashMonto = parseInt(crashParts[1].replace(/\./g, ''));
        if (isNaN(crashMonto) || crashMonto < 500) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Monto minimo: $500', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        if (crashMonto > 20000) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Monto maximo: $20.000', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        shopBuy(playerAuth, player.name, player.id, crashMonto, '!crash', 180000, function() {
            // Generar punto de crash con distribucion agresiva
            // 35% crash instantaneo (x1.0 - x1.5), 25% crash rapido (x1.5 - x2.5)
            // 25% crash medio (x2.5 - x4.0), 15% crash alto (x4.0 - x8.0)
            var crashRoll = Math.random();
            var crashPoint;
            if (crashRoll < 0.35) crashPoint = 1.0 + Math.random() * 0.5;
            else if (crashRoll < 0.60) crashPoint = 1.5 + Math.random() * 1.0;
            else if (crashRoll < 0.85) crashPoint = 2.5 + Math.random() * 1.5;
            else crashPoint = 4.0 + Math.random() * 4.0;
            botState.crashActive = {
                auth: playerAuth, name: player.name, playerId: player.id, monto: crashMonto,
                multiplier: 1.00, crashPoint: crashPoint, crashed: false, interval: null, ticks: 0
            };
            room.sendAnnouncement('🚀 CRASH iniciado por ' + player.name + ' (' + formatMoney(crashMonto) + ')!\nEscribe !crash para retirar!', null, 0x00BFFF, 'bold', 2);
            botState.crashActive.interval = setInterval(function() {
                if (!botState.crashActive) return;
                // Pausar durante explicaciones y durante noche de Impostor/Pistolero
                if (botState.gamePaused) return;
                try { if (IMPOSTOR && IMPOSTOR.isActive && IMPOSTOR.isActive()) return; } catch(e){}
                try { if (PISTOLERO && PISTOLERO.isActive && PISTOLERO.isActive()) return; } catch(e){}
                botState.crashActive.multiplier += 0.15 + Math.random() * 0.25;
                botState.crashActive.multiplier = parseFloat(botState.crashActive.multiplier.toFixed(2));
                if (botState.crashActive.multiplier >= botState.crashActive.crashPoint) {
                    // CRASH!
                    clearInterval(botState.crashActive.interval);
                    botState.crashActive.crashed = true;
                    room.sendAnnouncement('💥 CRASH en x' + botState.crashActive.multiplier.toFixed(2) + '! ' + botState.crashActive.name + ' perdio ' + formatMoney(botState.crashActive.monto), null, 0xFF0000, 'bold', 2);
                    botState.crashActive = null;
                } else {
                    botState.crashActive.ticks++;
                    // Solo mostrar mensaje cada 3 ticks para reducir spam
                    if (botState.crashActive.ticks % 3 === 0) {
                        room.sendAnnouncement('🚀 ' + botState.crashActive.name + ' x' + botState.crashActive.multiplier.toFixed(2) + ' ... escribe !crash para retirar!', null, 0xFFFF00);
                    }
                }
            }, 1500);
        });
        return false;
    }

    // !dados [monto] - Tirar dados (cooldown 30s)
    if (message.startsWith('!dados')) {
        if (_apuestasBloqueadas) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Espera a que termine la ronda actual', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        var dadosParts = message.split(' ');
        if (dadosParts.length < 2) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('🎲 Usa: !dados [monto]\n7+ = x2 | Doble = x3 | Doble 6 = x5', player.id, 0xFFFF00);
            return false;
        }
        var dadosMonto = parseInt(dadosParts[1].replace(/\./g, ''));
        if (isNaN(dadosMonto) || dadosMonto < 100) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Monto minimo: $100', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        if (dadosMonto > 20000) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Monto maximo: $20.000', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        shopBuy(playerAuth, player.name, player.id, dadosMonto, '!dados', 30000, function() {
            var d1 = Math.floor(Math.random() * 6) + 1;
            var d2 = Math.floor(Math.random() * 6) + 1;
            var suma = d1 + d2;
            var doble = d1 === d2;
            room.sendAnnouncement('🎲 ' + player.name + ' tira los dados...', null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold');
            setTimeout(function() {
                var dadosPremio = 0;
                var dadosMsg = '🎲 [' + d1 + '] [' + d2 + '] = ' + suma;
                if (d1 === 6 && d2 === 6) {
                    dadosPremio = dadosMonto * 4;
                    dadosMsg += '\n💎 DOBLE 6! x4 = ' + formatMoney(dadosPremio);
                } else if (suma === 7) {
                    dadosPremio = dadosMonto * 2;
                    dadosMsg += '\n✅ 7 exacto! x2 = ' + formatMoney(dadosPremio);
                } else if (suma === 12 || suma === 2) {
                    dadosPremio = dadosMonto * 3;
                    dadosMsg += '\n🎯 ' + (suma === 12 ? 'Maximo' : 'Minimo') + '! x3 = ' + formatMoney(dadosPremio);
                } else {
                    dadosMsg += '\n❌ Pierdes ' + formatMoney(dadosMonto);
                }
                if (dadosPremio > 0) {
                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(playerAuth, player.name, dadosPremio); } catch(e) {}
                }
                room.sendAnnouncement(dadosMsg, null, dadosPremio > 0 ? 0x00FF00 : 0xFF0000, 'bold', 2);
            }, 1500);
        });
        return false;
    }

    // !slots [monto] - Tragamonedas 777 (cooldown 30s)
    if (message.startsWith('!slots')) {
        if (_apuestasBloqueadas) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Espera a que termine la ronda actual', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        var slotsParts = message.split(' ');
        if (slotsParts.length < 2) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('🎰 Usa: !slots [monto]\nCombos: 777 = x50 | Triple = x10 | Doble = x3', player.id, 0xFFFF00);
            return false;
        }
        var slotsMonto = parseInt(slotsParts[1].replace(/\./g, ''));
        if (isNaN(slotsMonto) || slotsMonto < 100) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Monto minimo: $100', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        if (slotsMonto > 20000) { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Monto maximo: $20.000', player.id, 0xFF6600); return false; }
        shopBuy(playerAuth, player.name, player.id, slotsMonto, '!slots', 30000, function() {
            var slotsSymbols = ['🍒', '🍋', '🔔', '⭐', '💎', '7️⃣', '🍇', '🍊', '🍉'];
            var s1 = slotsSymbols[Math.floor(Math.random() * slotsSymbols.length)];
            var s2 = slotsSymbols[Math.floor(Math.random() * slotsSymbols.length)];
            var s3 = slotsSymbols[Math.floor(Math.random() * slotsSymbols.length)];
            room.sendAnnouncement('🎰 ' + player.name + ' jala la palanca...', null, 0xFFFF00, 'bold');
            setTimeout(function() {
                var slotsPremio = 0;
                var slotsMsg = '🎰 [ ' + s1 + ' | ' + s2 + ' | ' + s3 + ' ]';
                if (s1 === '7️⃣' && s2 === '7️⃣' && s3 === '7️⃣') {
                    slotsPremio = slotsMonto * 50;
                    slotsMsg += '\n🔥 JACKPOT 777!!! x50 = ' + formatMoney(slotsPremio);
                } else if (s1 === '💎' && s2 === '💎' && s3 === '💎') {
                    slotsPremio = slotsMonto * 20;
                    slotsMsg += '\n💎 TRIPLE DIAMANTE! x20 = ' + formatMoney(slotsPremio);
                } else if (s1 === s2 && s2 === s3) {
                    slotsPremio = slotsMonto * 5;
                    slotsMsg += '\n🎯 TRIPLE! x5 = ' + formatMoney(slotsPremio);
                } else if (s1 === s2 || s2 === s3) {
                    slotsPremio = Math.floor(slotsMonto * 1.5);
                    slotsMsg += '\n✅ PAR! x1.5 = ' + formatMoney(slotsPremio);
                } else {
                    slotsMsg += '\n❌ Pierdes ' + formatMoney(slotsMonto);
                }
                if (slotsPremio > 0) {
                    try { window.__dbAddBalance(playerAuth, player.name, slotsPremio); } catch(e) {}
                }
                room.sendAnnouncement(slotsMsg, null, slotsPremio > 0 ? 0x00FF00 : 0xFF0000, 'bold', 2);
            }, 2000);
        });
        return false;
    }

    // !toprich - Top 5 mas ricos (excluye creadores)
    if (message === '!toprich') {
        if (typeof window.__dbGetTopPlayers === 'function') {
            window.__dbGetTopPlayers('balance', 10).then(function(top) {
                if (top && top.length > 0) {
                    var filtered = top.filter(function(p) { return CREATOR_AUTHS.indexOf(p.auth) === -1; }).slice(0, 5);
                    if (filtered.length === 0) { room.sendAnnouncement('📊 No hay estadisticas aun.', player.id, 0xFFFF00); return; }
                    var msg = '💰 TOP 5 MAS RICOS:\n';
                    var medals = ['🥇','🥈','🥉','4️⃣','5️⃣'];
                    for (var i = 0; i < filtered.length; i++) {
                        msg += medals[i] + ' ' + (filtered[i].name || 'Desconocido') + ' - ' + formatMoney(filtered[i].balance || 0) + '\n';
                    }
                    room.sendAnnouncement(msg, player.id, 0xFFD700, 'bold');
                } else {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('📊 No hay estadisticas aun.', player.id, 0xFFFF00);
                }
            }).catch(function() { room.sendAnnouncement('❌ Error al cargar top.', player.id, 0xFF0000); });
        }
        return false;
    }

    // !topracha - Top 5 mejores rachas historicas
    if (message === '!topracha') {
        if (typeof window.__dbGetTopPlayers === 'function') {
            window.__dbGetTopPlayers('bestStreak', 5).then(function(top) {
                if (top && top.length > 0) {
                    var msg = '🔥 TOP 5 MEJORES RACHAS:\n';
                    var medals = ['🥇','🥈','🥉','4️⃣','5️⃣'];
                    for (var i = 0; i < top.length; i++) {
                        msg += medals[i] + ' ' + (top[i].name || 'Desconocido') + ' - ' + (top[i].bestStreak || 0) + ' victorias seguidas\n';
                    }
                    room.sendAnnouncement(msg, player.id, 0xFFD700, 'bold');
                } else {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('📊 No hay estadisticas aun.', player.id, 0xFFFF00);
                }
            }).catch(function() { room.sendAnnouncement('❌ Error al cargar top.', player.id, 0xFF0000); });
        }
        return false;
    }

    // !topgeis - Top 5 que mas veces les ha tocado gay
    if (message === '!topgeis') {
        if (typeof window.__dbGetTopPlayers === 'function') {
            window.__dbGetTopPlayers('gayCount', 5).then(function(top) {
                if (top && top.length > 0) {
                    var msg = '🌈 TOP 5 MAS GEIS:\n';
                    var medals = ['🥇','🥈','🥉','4️⃣','5️⃣'];
                    for (var i = 0; i < top.length; i++) {
                        msg += medals[i] + ' ' + (top[i].name || 'Desconocido') + ' - ' + (top[i].gayCount || 0) + ' veces\n';
                    }
                    room.sendAnnouncement(msg, player.id, 0xFF69B4, 'bold');
                } else {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('📊 No hay estadisticas aun.', player.id, 0xFFFF00);
                }
            }).catch(function() { room.sendAnnouncement('❌ Error al cargar top.', player.id, 0xFF0000); });
        }
        return false;
    }

    // !topkick - Top 5 mas kickeados
    if (message === '!topkick') {
        if (typeof window.__dbGetTopPlayers === 'function') {
            window.__dbGetTopPlayers('kickCount', 5).then(function(top) {
                if (top && top.length > 0) {
                    var msg = '👢 TOP 5 MAS KICKEADOS:\n';
                    var medals = ['🥇','🥈','🥉','4️⃣','5️⃣'];
                    for (var i = 0; i < top.length; i++) {
                        msg += medals[i] + ' ' + (top[i].name || 'Desconocido') + ' - ' + (top[i].kickCount || 0) + ' kicks\n';
                    }
                    room.sendAnnouncement(msg, player.id, 0xFF6600, 'bold');
                } else {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('📊 No hay estadisticas aun.', player.id, 0xFFFF00);
                }
            }).catch(function() { room.sendAnnouncement('❌ Error al cargar top.', player.id, 0xFF0000); });
        }
        return false;
    }

    // !topban - Top 5 mas baneados
    if (message === '!topban') {
        if (typeof window.__dbGetTopPlayers === 'function') {
            window.__dbGetTopPlayers('banCount', 5).then(function(top) {
                if (top && top.length > 0) {
                    var msg = '🔨 TOP 5 MAS BANEADOS:\n';
                    var medals = ['🥇','🥈','🥉','4️⃣','5️⃣'];
                    for (var i = 0; i < top.length; i++) {
                        msg += medals[i] + ' ' + (top[i].name || 'Desconocido') + ' - ' + (top[i].banCount || 0) + ' bans\n';
                    }
                    room.sendAnnouncement(msg, player.id, 0xFF0000, 'bold');
                } else {
                    room.sendAnnouncement('📊 No hay estadisticas aun.', player.id, 0xFFFF00);
                }
            }).catch(function() { room.sendAnnouncement('❌ Error al cargar top.', player.id, 0xFF0000); });
        }
        return false;
    }

    // ============================================
    // COMANDO !fix - Votación para reiniciar
    // ============================================
    if (message === '!fix') {
        var now = Date.now();
        // Solo se puede usar si hay un juego activo
        if (!botState.gameActive) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ No hay juego activo para reiniciar', player.id, 0xFF6600);
            return false;
        }
        // Cooldown global de 5 minutos
        if (now < botState.fixCooldown) {
            var wait = Math.ceil((botState.fixCooldown - now) / 1000);
            room.sendAnnouncement('⏳ !fix en cooldown. Espera ' + wait + 's', player.id, 0xFF6600);
            return false;
        }
        // Cooldown individual de 30s (evitar spam)
        var voterAuth = getAuth(player);
        if (!voterAuth) { return false; }
        if (!botState.fixPlayerCooldowns) botState.fixPlayerCooldowns = {};
        if (botState.fixPlayerCooldowns[voterAuth] && now - botState.fixPlayerCooldowns[voterAuth] < 30000) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('⏳ Ya votaste, espera un momento', player.id, 0xFF6600);
            return false;
        }
        botState.fixPlayerCooldowns[voterAuth] = now;
        // Limpiar votos expirados (>45s) y registrar voto POR AUTH (no por ID)
        var validVotes = {};
        for (var vAuth in botState.fixVotes) {
            if (now - botState.fixVotes[vAuth] < 45000) validVotes[vAuth] = botState.fixVotes[vAuth];
        }
        validVotes[voterAuth] = now;
        botState.fixVotes = validVotes;

        var playerCount = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; }).length;
        // Necesita 70% de los jugadores (mínimo 3 votos)
        var needed = Math.max(3, Math.ceil(playerCount * 0.7));
        var currentVotes = Object.keys(botState.fixVotes).length;

        if (currentVotes >= needed) {
            room.sendAnnouncement('🔧 !fix aprobado (' + currentVotes + '/' + needed + '). Reiniciando...', null, 0x00FF00, 'bold', 2);
            botState.fixVotes = {};
            botState.fixPlayerCooldowns = {};
            botState.fixCooldown = now + 300000;
            forceStopAllGames();
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
        } else {
            room.sendAnnouncement('🔧 !fix voto: ' + currentVotes + '/' + needed + ' (faltan ' + (needed - currentVotes) + ')', null, 0xFFFF00);
        }
        return false;
    }

    return true;
};

room.onGameStart = function() {
    console.log("🎮 Juego iniciado");
    botState.gamePaused = false;
    // Inicializar actividad AFK de todos los jugadores en equipo
    var now = Date.now();
    var ps = room.getPlayerList();
    botState.afkLastActivity = {};
    for (var i = 0; i < ps.length; i++) {
        if (ps[i].id !== 0 && ps[i].team !== 0) {
            botState.afkLastActivity[ps[i].id] = now;
        }
    }
};

room.onGameStop = function() {
    console.log("⏹️ Juego detenido");
    botState.gamePaused = false;
};

room.onGamePause = function() {
    botState.gamePaused = true;
};

room.onGameUnpause = function() {
    botState.gamePaused = false;
    // Resetear actividad AFK al despausar (para no acumular tiempo de pausa)
    var now = Date.now();
    for (var id in botState.afkLastActivity) {
        botState.afkLastActivity[id] = now;
    }
};

// ============================================
// SAFETY: detectar juegos atascados sin jugadores en equipo
// ============================================
var _safetyStuckSince = null;
setInterval(function() {
    if (!botState.gameActive) { _safetyStuckSince = null; return; }
    // No interferir con juegos que ponen jugadores en espectador (es normal)
    if (LUCKY.isActive() || (LUCKY_HELL && LUCKY_HELL.isActive && LUCKY_HELL.isActive()) || (LUCKY_DIOS && LUCKY_DIOS.isActive && LUCKY_DIOS.isActive()) || (IMPOSTOR && IMPOSTOR.isActive && IMPOSTOR.isActive()) || (PISTOLERO && PISTOLERO.isActive && PISTOLERO.isActive())) {
        _safetyStuckSince = null;
        return;
    }
    var activePlayers = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && p.team !== 0; });
    if (activePlayers.length === 0) {
        if (!_safetyStuckSince) {
            _safetyStuckSince = Date.now();
        } else if (Date.now() - _safetyStuckSince > 15000) {
            console.log('⚠️ SAFETY: juego activo sin jugadores en equipo por 15s. Forzando reinicio.');
            room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ Juego atascado detectado. Reiniciando...', null, 0xFF6600, 'bold');
            forceStopAllGames();
            _safetyStuckSince = null;
            setTimeout(checkAndStart, 3000);
        }
    } else {
        _safetyStuckSince = null;
    }
}, 5000);

// ============================================
// RECORDATORIO PERIODICO: !fix para bugs
// ============================================
setInterval(function() {
    if (!botState.gameActive) return;
    var playerCount = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0; }).length;
    if (playerCount < 2) return;
    room.sendAnnouncement('💡 Si el juego se bugeo, escribe !fix para votar un reinicio', null, 0x999999);
}, 90000);

// ============================================
// SISTEMA AFK: auto-kick por inactividad (25 segundos sin presionar tecla)
// ============================================
room.onPlayerActivity = function(player) {
    botState.afkLastActivity[player.id] = Date.now();
    delete botState.afkWarned[player.id];
};

setInterval(function() {
    if (botState.gamePaused) return;
    if (!botState.gameActive) return;

    // No kickear AFK en juegos basados en chat (no requieren movimiento)
    // Trivia, impostor, pistolero, GOT, number chairs, pinball, zombie run
    var skipAFK = false;
    try { if (IMPOSTOR && IMPOSTOR.isActive && IMPOSTOR.isActive()) skipAFK = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (PISTOLERO && PISTOLERO.isActive && PISTOLERO.isActive()) skipAFK = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (TRIVIA && TRIVIA.isActive && TRIVIA.isActive()) skipAFK = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (GOT && GOT.isActive && GOT.isActive()) skipAFK = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (NUMBERCHAIRS && NUMBERCHAIRS.isActive && NUMBERCHAIRS.isActive()) skipAFK = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (PINBALL_ROULETTE && PINBALL_ROULETTE.isActive && PINBALL_ROULETTE.isActive()) skipAFK = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (ZOMBIE_RUN && ZOMBIE_RUN.isActive && ZOMBIE_RUN.isActive()) skipAFK = true; } catch(e){}
    if (skipAFK) {
        var resetNow = Date.now();
        var resetP = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && p.team !== 0; });
        for (var ri = 0; ri < resetP.length; ri++) {
            botState.afkLastActivity[resetP[ri].id] = resetNow;
        }
        return;
    }

    // No kickear AFK durante juicio público
    if (botState.banVoteActive) return;

    var now = Date.now();
    var players = room.getPlayerList().filter(function(p) { return p.id !== 0 && p.team !== 0; });

    players.forEach(function(p) {
        if (!botState.afkLastActivity[p.id]) {
            botState.afkLastActivity[p.id] = now;
            return;
        }

        var inactiveMs = now - botState.afkLastActivity[p.id];
        // 20s sin presionar tecla = advertencia
        if (inactiveMs >= 20000 && inactiveMs < 25000 && !botState.afkWarned[p.id]) {
            botState.afkWarned[p.id] = true;
            try { room.sendAnnouncement('⚠️ ' + p.name + ' ¡Presiona una tecla o serás kickeado por AFK!', p.id, 0xFF6600); } catch(e) {}
        }
        if (inactiveMs >= 25000) { // 25 segundos sin presionar tecla = kick
            try {
                room.sendAnnouncement('⏰ ' + p.name + ' fue kickeado por AFK', null, 0xFF6600);
                room.kickPlayer(p.id, 'AFK - sin actividad', false);
            } catch(e) {}
            delete botState.afkLastActivity[p.id];
            delete botState.afkWarned[p.id];
        }
    });

    // Limpiar entradas de jugadores que ya no están en equipo
    var activeIds = players.map(function(p) { return p.id; });
    for (var pid in botState.afkLastActivity) {
        if (activeIds.indexOf(parseInt(pid)) === -1) {
            delete botState.afkLastActivity[pid];
        }
    }
}, 5000);

// ============================================
// INICIO
// ============================================

setTimeout(function() {
    room.sendAnnouncement(
        "🎮 Bienvenidos a la Sala de Minijuegos 🎮\n" +
        "Los minijuegos se ejecutan automáticamente",
        null,
        0x00FF00,
        "bold",
        2
    );
    checkAndStart();
}, 5000);
